Key: Standard Lead Matching Rule uses multi-algorithm fuzzy matching (Jaro-Winkler, Metaphone 3); Data Import Wizard supports only single-field exact-match dedup; Web-to-Lead submissions bypass blocking rules silently — use Alert-only mode; 5-active-rules-per-object limit; high-volume orgs typically require third-party tools for fuzzy cross-object Lead-to-Contact dedup. Local data-migration-planning skill documents sequencing pattern already. |
| DONE | product-catalog-data-model | Product and Pricebook data model: PricebookEntry management, product hierarchies, data loading sequence, bulk loading. | DONE | sales-reporting-data-model | Sales data model for reporting: opportunity snapshots, trending reports, custom report types for pipeline analysis. Key: Two complementary mechanisms — Historical Trend Reporting (declarative, 3-4 months retention, up to 8 tracked fields, requires early activation) and Reporting Snapshots (freeze report data to custom object on schedule, 2,000 source row cap, unlimited history); Custom Report Types support 4-object chains and 'without' joins for exception/gap analysis. No duplicate. |
| DONE | territory-data-alignment | Territory alignment data: account-territory assignments, territory history, bulk reassignment, territory coverage analysis. NOT for ETM configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Territory Management 2.0 Data Model; ObjectTerritory2Association Object Reference; Track Historical User Assignments — help.salesforce.com]. Key: Account-territory via ObjectTerritory2Association (queryable/insertable via API), user-territory via UserTerritory2Association; Territory2ModelHistory and Track Territory Assignment History feature (GA Spring '25) enable audit; coverage analysis requires SOQL across ObjectTerritory2Association, Territory2, Account with AssociationCause filter (manual vs rule-driven). No duplicate. |

## Phase 3 — Service Cloud

### Service Cloud × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | case-management-setup | Case settings, support processes, case teams, case comments, case feeds, web-to-case, case auto-response. NOT for case assignment rules (use assignment-rules). | Researched 2026-04-05. Sources: [help.salesforce.com — Email-to-Case Limits; Assignment/Auto-Response/Escalation Rule Limits; Set Up Entitlements and Milestones]. Key: Full config layer: queues (pool-based ownership), assignment rules (one active, first-match-wins, up to 3,000 entries, auto-runs for Email-to-Case/Web-to-Case but requires explicit header for API/Data Loader), escalation rules (one active, hourly engine cadence — not real-time, business hours must be configured or clock runs 24/7), auto-response (fires ONLY when assignment rule also fires — common false assumption), Email-to-Case (25 MB inbound limit, body truncated at 32k chars, thread ID misconfiguration creates dup cases), Web-to-Case (50,000 pending request hard limit, no native field validation, contact auto-populated only if email matches), case teams (role-based, grants case access independent of org sharing), entitlements/milestones (enable in Setup first, milestones require entitlement process, add entitlement templates to products via Classic only). Critical gotchas: deactivating/reactivating escalation rule can trigger wave of immediate escalations; same subject+body Email-to-Case = infinite email loop; deleted queues orphan cases. LLM anti-patterns: claiming auto-response is independent of assignment rules; asserting sub-hour escalation precision; equating entitlements with escalation rules. No duplicate. |
| DONE | omni-channel-routing-setup | Omni-Channel routing configuration: queue-based vs skills-based routing, agent capacity, presence statuses, routing logic. NOT for OmniStudio. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help - Routing Model Options for Service Cloud Omni-Channel; SF Help - Skills-Based vs Queue-Based Routing; Omni-Channel for Administrators PDF; Trailhead - Queue-Based Routing Setup]. Key: Two primary routing models: queue-based (Least Active or Most Available assignment) and skills-based (matching agents by required skill competencies via Service Resource skill assignments and routing rules); capacity managed via points-based tab model or status-based capacity model. Presence statuses must be configured per service channel; skills-based requires enabling feature, creating Skills objects, assigning to Service Resources, and defining Skills-Based Routing Rules. No duplicate. |
| DONE | entitlements-and-milestones | Entitlement process setup: milestone types, milestone actions, entitlement verification, SLA tracking, business hours. NOT for case escalation rules. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help - Set Up and Manage Entitlements and Milestones; SF Help - Milestone Actions; SF Help - Business Hours in Entitlement Management; SF Ben - Complete Guide]. Key: Entitlement processes contain milestones with three recurrence types (No Recurrence, Sequential, Independent) and three action categories (Success, Warning, Violation) supporting email alerts, task creation, and field updates; milestone timers run/pause based on configured business hours at process or individual milestone level (individual overrides process-level). Entitlement templates can auto-create entitlements on product purchase but require Classic to attach templates to products; in Lightning, Flow automation needed. No duplicate. |
| DONE | knowledge-base-administration | Salesforce Knowledge setup: article types, data categories, publishing workflow, Lightning Knowledge, approval processes. NOT for Knowledge in Experience Cloud. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help - Set Up Lightning Knowledge; SF Help - Workflow and Approvals for Articles; Lightning Knowledge Guide PDF; SF Help - Record Type Considerations; SF Help - Data Categories]. Key: Lightning Knowledge replaces Classic article types with standard record types on single Knowledge__kav object - once enabled cannot be disabled, making migration irreversible. Data Categories serve dual purpose: content organization via hierarchical Category Groups and access control via role/profile/permission-set visibility (user must have visibility to at least one category in every group assigned to article). Publishing workflow uses three native statuses (Draft, Published, Archived) plus admin-customizable Validation Status picklist; approval processes can be layered on top. No duplicate. |
| DONE | email-to-case-configuration | Email-to-Case and On-Demand Email-to-Case setup: routing addresses, email threading, attachment handling, auto-response. NOT for email templates. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help - Set Up Email-to-Case; SF Help - Email-to-Case Limits and Limitations; astreait.com - Email-to-Case vs On-Demand]. Key: Standard Email-to-Case requires agent behind company firewall keeping email traffic internal; On-Demand uses Apex Email Services with no agent required but routes traffic externally and consumes API calls. Both support up to 25MB total email size but On-Demand caps individual attachments at 10MB. Threading works via Lightning tokens in outgoing email body/subject matched on customer reply to associate back to originating case; routing addresses map inbound emails to cases with configurable auto-response rules, priority, and team assignment. No duplicate. |
| DONE | service-console-configuration | Service Console app setup: utility bar, split view, macros, quick text, keyboard shortcuts, console navigation. NOT for generic Lightning app setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help - Keyboard Shortcuts for Lightning Console Apps; Trailhead - Set Up the Lightning Service Console; SF Help - Features Available in Lightning Console Apps]. Key: Service Console is Lightning App with Console Navigation (not Standard) enabling split view - side-panel list view persisting while agents work records in workspace tabs and subtabs. Utility bar configured per-app via App Manager supports Macros, History, Omni-Channel, Open CTI Softphone; macros automate multi-step repetitive actions with single click. Quick Text provides reusable message snippets. Keyboard shortcuts configurable at console app level covering tab navigation, record opening, macro execution; navigation rules define how each object opens (workspace tab vs subtab). No duplicate. |
| DONE | messaging-and-chat-setup | Messaging for In-App and Web, Chat configuration: pre-chat forms, chat routing, embedded service deployment, queues. NOT for Agentforce bots. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Configure an Enhanced Web Chat Deployment — help.salesforce.com; Embedded Chat Developer Guide Spring '26; Route Messaging Sessions with Omni-Channel Flows]. Key: MIAW replaces legacy Live Agent/Snap-ins; setup requires Messaging Channel, Embedded Service Deployment, CORS/CSP Trusted Sites for every widget domain, and Omni-Channel routing via Queue or Flow with fallback; pre-chat fields defined on Messaging Channel record; Status-Based capacity model recommended. No duplicate. |
| DONE | service-cloud-voice-setup | Service Cloud Voice configuration: Amazon Connect integration, call routing, transcription, after-call work, recording. NOT for CTI adapter development. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Set Up Service Cloud Voice with Amazon Connect — help.salesforce.com; Configure Call Transcription; Configure After Conversation Work Time; Service Cloud Voice Best Practice Guide]. Key: Guided wizard provisions Amazon Connect instance from Setup handling OAuth, phone numbers, contact flows, and Omni-Channel service channel; prereqs: Omni-Channel enabled, custom domain, Voice add-on license plus Contact Center permission sets; real-time transcription requires enabling live media streaming in Connect instance; ACW via After Conversation Work Time holds agent in wrap-up presence status. No duplicate. |

### Service Cloud × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | sla-design-and-escalation-matrix | SLA tier design: escalation matrix documentation, response/resolution time requirements, business hours alignment. NOT for entitlement configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce Help — Entitlements and Milestones; local skills/architect/service-cloud-architecture; local skills/admin/case-management-setup]. Key: SLA enforcement via Entitlement Processes with Milestones that fire actions at configurable percentage thresholds (50%/75%/90%/100%); business hours must be attached to both entitlement processes AND escalation rule entries or elapsed time is measured 24/7; no existing skill covers the design artifact layer (escalation matrix document, tier definition table, business hours mapping). No duplicate. |
| DONE | knowledge-taxonomy-design | Knowledge article taxonomy: data category hierarchy, article lifecycle, content gap analysis, authoring guidelines. NOT for Knowledge admin setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Knowledge Data Categories Best Practices — help.salesforce.com; Work with Data Categories; Archive Articles and Translations; KCS Methodology — Trailhead]. Key: Up to 5 Data Category Groups (3 active by default), 5 hierarchy levels, 100 categories per group; articles move through Draft → Published → Archived with validation-status gating; content gap analysis via Search Activity Gaps dashboard and KCS Solve/Evolve Loop practices embedding article creation into case resolution. No duplicate. |
| DONE | agent-console-requirements | Service console requirements: agent workflow mapping, case handling process, macro requirements, screen layouts. NOT for console configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Trailhead: Set Up Lightning Service Console; Customize Lightning Service Console Pages; Lightning Service Console Intro — help.salesforce.com]. Key: Tabbed multi-panel workspace requiring Service Cloud license and console permission sets; case pages use Pinned Header template with Highlights Panel, Knowledge Accordion, Chatter; split-view navigation where cases open as account subtabs; Macros are required console utility alongside History and Open CTI Softphone for agent productivity. No duplicate. |
| DONE | case-deflection-strategy | Self-service strategy: knowledge article surfacing, chatbot requirements, case deflection metrics, ROI measurement. NOT for Experience Cloud setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Deflect Cases with Self-Service — help.salesforce.com; Einstein Conversation Mining for Case Deflection; AI for Admins: Einstein Bots Success]. Key: Targets high-frequency low-complexity contact reasons identified via Einstein Conversation Mining; primary KPIs are deflection rate and goal completion rate; documented 27% average deflection rates and 198% ROI; Knowledge article quality and data category hygiene are critical prerequisites for any deflection program. No duplicate. |
| DONE | customer-effort-scoring | Customer effort metrics: CSAT design, survey requirements, service quality measurement, NPS integration. NOT for custom survey implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce Feedback Management Overview; Set Up Customer Feedback Survey; Service Insights CSAT Dashboard — help.salesforce.com]. Key: CSAT (1-5 scale), NPS (0-10 auto-bucketed Detractor/Passive/Promoter), and CES supported natively via Salesforce Surveys (Feedback Management license) with Flow-triggered invitations; CES best triggered within 1 hour of case closure; existing salesforce-surveys skill covers technical build — this skill focuses on measurement strategy, metric selection, and reporting KPI integration. No duplicate. |

### Service Cloud × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | case-trigger-patterns | Apex triggers for Case: auto-assignment overrides, entitlement verification, SLA calculation, case merge handling. NOT for generic trigger patterns (use trigger-framework). | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Assignment Rule Header — REST API Dev Guide; Run Case Assignment Rule from Apex — help.salesforce.com; Triggers and Merge Statements — Apex Dev Guide; Entitlement Implementation Guide]. Key: Must explicitly invoke assignment rules via Database.DmlOptions.AssignmentRuleHeader (DML from Apex bypasses rules by default); entitlement auto-association requires Before Insert/Update trigger querying EntitlementContact; merge events fire delete triggers with MasterRecordId on losing records; closing case does not auto-complete milestones. No duplicate. |
| DONE | knowledge-article-lwc | Custom Lightning components for Knowledge: article display, search, recommendation widgets, feedback collection. NOT for standard Knowledge setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Knowledge with SOQL and SOSL — developer.salesforce.com; Knowledge Developer Guide Spring '26; KnowledgeArticleBodyContent GitHub component; Custom Knowledge LWC — salesforcecodex.com]. Key: Query Knowledge__kav via Apex wired to SOQL/SOSL — no dedicated platform wire adapter for Knowledge article content; all retrieval through @wire(getRecord) or @AuraEnabled(cacheable=true) methods; Experience Cloud guest access requires data category visibility and sharing settings; feedback/voting via custom Apex endpoints. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cti-adapter-development | CTI integration: Open CTI API, softphone panel, click-to-dial, screen pop, call logging via Apex, adapter patterns. NOT for Service Cloud Voice admin. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Open CTI Developer Guide — Get Started; Open CTI Demo Adapter; onClickToDial for Lightning; lightning-click-to-dial component]. Key: Browser-based JavaScript API for CTI integration; adapter defined by callcenter.xml definition file registered as Lightning utility item; core methods: enableClickToDial, onClickToDial, screenPop, setSoftphonePanelHeight, saveLog; call logging creates closed Task activities; no existing local skill covers this topic. No duplicate. |
| DONE | omni-channel-custom-routing | Custom Omni-Channel routing via Apex: PendingServiceRouting, custom skills matching, overflow handling, priority routing. NOT for admin routing setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [PendingServiceRouting Object Reference; SkillRequirement Object Reference; How Skills-Based Routing Works — help.salesforce.com]. Key: Custom routing requires mandatory three-DML sequence: insert PendingServiceRouting (with RoutingType=SkillsBased, IsReadyForRouting=false), associate SkillRequirement records, then flip IsReadyForRouting=true; overflow via skill relaxation dropping IsAdditionalSkill=true skills after timeout; common pitfalls: hardcoding ServiceChannelId (breaks across sandboxes), querying Skill by DeveloperName in loops. No duplicate. |
| DONE | entitlement-apex-hooks | Entitlement process Apex extension: custom milestone completion, SLA breach notifications, case status automation. NOT for admin entitlement setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Auto-Complete Case Milestones — help.salesforce.com; CaseMilestone Field Writability; Entitlements Implementation Guide Spring '26]. Key: CaseMilestone.IsCompleted is read-only — set indirectly by writing CompletionDate=System.now() in after-update trigger filtered by MilestoneType.Name; SlaExitDate is system-managed and cannot be written by Apex; no native Apex callback for milestone violation — must poll CaseMilestone where IsViolated=true or TargetDate < NOW() AND CompletionDate=null. No duplicate. |
| DONE | service-cloud-rest-api | Service Cloud specific REST APIs: Case API patterns, Knowledge API, Chat REST API, Messaging API endpoints. NOT for generic REST API. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Knowledge REST APIs Developer Guide; Enhanced Chat API Overview; Chat REST API Developer Guide — developer.salesforce.com]. Key: Two distinct API families — legacy Chat REST API (retiring Feb 14, 2026) and replacement Enhanced Chat API (MIAW); Knowledge articles via /knowledgeManagement/ (authoring) and /support/knowledgeWithSEO/ (guest retrieval) with data category filtering and URL-name lookup (API v44+); no existing local skill covers unified Service Cloud REST API patterns. No duplicate. |

### Service Cloud × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | case-history-migration | Migrating historical case data: case comments, email messages, attachments, activity history, status mapping. NOT for generic data migration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Gluon Digital — Migrating Email Messages with Attachments; CaseComment Object Reference; ContentVersion/ContentDocumentLink Object References — developer.salesforce.com]. Key: Strict load order: Case → CaseComment → EmailMessage → EmailMessageRelation → ContentVersion → ContentDocumentLink; setting EmailMessage Status='3' (Sent) permanently locks record read-only with no override; ContentDocumentLink does not support Bulk API batching; CaseHistory is system-generated and not insertable. No duplicate. |
| DONE | knowledge-article-import | Importing Knowledge articles: CSV import, article field mapping, category assignment, publishing status, bulk loading. NOT for Knowledge admin setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Import External Content into Salesforce Knowledge — help.salesforce.com; Create CSV for Article Import; Lightning Knowledge Guide Spring '26]. Key: Requires ZIP file (max 20 MB) with CSV, .properties file, and optional HTML/assets folder; CSV columns: Title, URLName, RecordTypeId, IsMasterLanguage, Language, channels, datacategorygroup columns with +-delimited category names; articles always land in Draft status — no publish-on-import option; bulk publishing requires separate post-import step via list views or API. No duplicate. |
| DONE | service-metrics-data-model | Service reporting data model: case duration calculations, SLA compliance metrics, agent performance data, MTTR. NOT for CRM Analytics. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Track Service Metrics — help.salesforce.com; CaseMilestone Object Reference; Entitlements and Milestones Guide — Salesforce Ben]. Key: Three primary objects: Case (CreatedDate, ClosedDate), Entitlement (SLA tier linkage), CaseMilestone (StartDate, TargetDate, CompletionDate, IsCompleted, IsViolated, ElapsedTimeInMins); MTTR has no native single field — derive via formula or BusinessHours.diff(); critical gotcha: IsViolated can be true even when CompletionDate is set if completion was after TargetDate. No duplicate. |
| DONE | omni-channel-reporting-data | Omni-Channel analytics data: agent work records, queue metrics, capacity utilization, wait time reporting. NOT for admin routing setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Built 2026-04-06. |
| DONE | service-data-archival | Case archival strategies: email message cleanup, attachment management, compliance retention, storage optimization. NOT for generic data archival. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Email-to-Case Considerations — help.salesforce.com; Store Data Externally with Legacy Salesforce Archive; Create Retention Policies]. Key: EmailMessage records are primary storage driver distinct from ContentDocument file storage; ContentDocument/ContentVersion archival is separate pipeline — tools move case data but leave files unlinked unless explicitly configured; compliance-safe archival must coordinate three deletion sequences (Case → EmailMessage → ContentDocument/ContentDocumentLink) in dependency order with legal-hold exemptions. No duplicate. |

## Phase 4 — Experience Cloud

### Experience Cloud × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | experience-cloud-site-setup | Site creation: template selection (LWR vs Aura), branding, navigation menus, domain configuration, page builder. NOT for internal Lightning apps. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [LWR Sites for Experience Cloud v66.0 Spring 26; SF Help - Custom Domain for Experience Cloud; SF Help - Experience Builder]. Key: LWR templates (Build Your Own LWR and Microsite LWR) use LWC exclusively with superior performance via publish-time freezing and HTTP caching; legacy Aura-based Build Your Own template supports both Aura and LWC but lacks performance optimizations - template choice is permanent post-creation (changing requires recreation). LWR branding uses --dxp CSS styling hooks and branding sets; custom domain pattern MyDomainName.my.site.com; LWR sites support clean custom URL paths (no /s prefix) unlike Aura sites. Editions: Enterprise, Performance, Unlimited, Developer. No duplicate. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-member-management | Member profiles: external user licensing, registration flows, login page customization, self-registration. NOT for internal user management. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Add Members to Experience Cloud Site — help.salesforce.com; Configure Self-Registration; ConfigurableSelfRegHandler — Apex Reference; Experience Cloud Licenses]. Key: External users require Customer Community, Customer Community Plus, Partner Community, or External Identity license — profile tied to one license type cannot be assigned to different license user; self-registration needs default account, profile, and either declarative Configurable Self-Reg page or custom Apex Auth.ConfigurableSelfRegHandler; login page branding via Experience Builder Login and Registration settings. No duplicate. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-cms-content | CMS workspace setup: content types, content publishing, audience targeting, content scheduling, managed content. NOT for Knowledge articles. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce CMS and Digital Experiences App — help.salesforce.com; Types of CMS Content; CMS Developer Guide; Content Publication Schedules]. Key: CMS workspaces (via Digital Experiences app) organize content creation, versioning, and publishing including standard types (news, banners, images) and custom content types via Metadata/Tooling API; content published to Experience Builder sites through CMS channels with scheduling and audience targeting per variant; no existing local skill covers native CMS workspace authoring. No duplicate. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-guest-access | Guest user profile configuration: public access settings, unauthenticated page design, object-level security review. NOT for authenticated user features. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Securely Share Experience Cloud Sites with Guest Users; Secure Guest Users Sharing Settings; Give Secure Access to Unauthenticated Users — help.salesforce.com; Experience Cloud Developer Guide]. Key: Each site has exactly one guest user profile; guiding principle is least-privilege — disable Allow guest users to access public APIs and API Enabled, set external OWD to Private, grant access only through explicit sharing rules. Overlap note: strong overlap with existing security/guest-user-security skill — differentiate by focusing on public page design and page-level access configuration in Experience Builder rather than security hardening. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-moderation | Content moderation setup: flagging rules, reputation system, member management, content approval workflows. NOT for CMS content publishing. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Experience Cloud Site Moderation Strategies — help.salesforce.com; Create Rules to Moderate; Set Up Reputation Levels/Points; Connect REST API Moderation Resources]. Key: Three layered capabilities: (1) rule-based automated moderation with keyword/member criteria triggering Block/Replace/Flag/Review actions; (2) reputation system with up to 10 configurable levels and point thresholds for member actions; (3) moderation queue with Moderate Experiences Feeds permission for reviewing flagged items — content pending Review is hidden from all but author and moderators until approved. No duplicate. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-seo-settings | SEO configuration for Experience Cloud sites: page titles, meta descriptions, URL structure, robots.txt, sitemap. NOT for external SEO tools. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SEO for Experience Builder Sites — help.salesforce.com; SEO Page Properties; Create Custom robots.txt; Advanced Communities SEO guide]. Key: Per-page SEO properties (title, meta description, noindex) configured in Experience Builder page properties panel; sitemap.xml auto-generates from pages and objects guest profile can read (Knowledge articles require topic assignment); custom robots.txt implemented as VF page with contentType=text/plain — sites sharing custom domain via subpaths share single robots.txt file; SEO features only active on production orgs. No duplicate. |

### Experience Cloud × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `lwc`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | lwr-site-development | LWR (Lightning Web Runtime) site development: custom themes, LWC for Experience Cloud, build configuration. NOT for Aura-based communities. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [LWR Sites for Experience Cloud developer guide v66.0 Spring '26 — local knowledge/imports/exp-cloud-lwr.md; Build Your Own (LWR) template documentation]. Key: Two templates — Build Your Own (LWR) and Microsite (LWR) — powered exclusively by LWC with Lightning Web Security (not Locker); publish-time-freeze/static-serving model requires explicit republish to deploy changes; custom theming via --dxp CSS styling hooks and lightningCommunity__Theme_Layout targets; no support for Aura components, default theme management, app-level events, or Chatter feeds. No duplicate. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-lwc-components | Building custom LWC for Experience Cloud: data access patterns, guest user Apex, community context, navigation. NOT for internal LWC. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [LWC Dev Guide — Configure Component for Experience Builder; LWC Dev Guide — Current Community; LWC Dev Guide — Secure Apex Classes; LWR Sites — Lightning Navigation]. Key: Components import community context via @salesforce/community/Id and basePath, detect guest via @salesforce/user/isGuest — these modules restrict to Experience Builder targets only. Guest-accessible Apex must use 'with sharing'; @AuraEnabled methods require explicit profile/permission-set access for guest and authenticated users. LWR uses lightning/navigation while Aura uses community-specific pageReference types — not interchangeable. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-authentication | Custom login flows: social sign-on, self-registration, passwordless login, SSO for external users, auth providers. NOT for internal SSO. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Authenticate Experience Cloud Site Users; SF Help — Passwordless Login; SF Help — Headless Passwordless Login Settings; SF Dev — HeadlessSelfRegistrationHandler Interface]. Key: Supports social login via auth providers (OIDC/SAML), self-registration with Apex RegistrationHandler or ConfigurableSelfRegHandler, and passwordless login via OTP backed by HeadlessPasswordlessLogin API. Headless flows require HeadlessUserDiscoveryHandler and HeadlessSelfRegistrationHandler — distinct from standard RegistrationHandler. Custom login pages are VF for Aura sites and LWC for LWR sites. |
| DONE | headless-experience-cloud | Headless CMS API: content delivery API, building custom frontends against Experience Cloud data, channel access. NOT for standard site building. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — CMS Developer Guide: Display CMS Content in Other Systems; Connect REST API — CMS Delivery Content; SF Dev Blog — Build Static Sites with SF CMS Headless APIs]. Key: Salesforce CMS exposes content via Connect REST API /connect/cms/delivery/channels/{channelId}/contents — channel ID is the gateway. Public channels need no auth; authenticated channels require OAuth connected app. CMS Connect (federating 3rd-party CMS into Experience Builder) is separate from the headless delivery API (delivering SF CMS content to external frontends). |
| DONE | experience-cloud-api-access | API access for community users: guest user API limits, external user OAuth scopes, sharing enforcement. NOT for internal API security. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Experience Cloud License Limitations; SF Help — Securely Share Sites with Guest Users; SF Help — OAuth 2.0 for First-Party Apps; Local: security/guest-user-security]. Key: Guest users have no named session and cannot use OAuth — all Apex must run with sharing against guest profile FLS. Customer Community licenses cannot access REST/SOAP API directly; Customer Community Plus and Partner Community can, subject to sharing rules and external OWDs. Permission sets can grant guest users Apex class access but FLS on guest profile is the hard enforcement boundary. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-search-customization | Customizing search in Experience Cloud: federated search, search result components, search scope, global search. NOT for SOSL queries. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Federated Search in Experience Cloud; SF Help — Customize Search in Experience Cloud; SF Help — Search Behavior in Experience Cloud]. Key: Search scope is per-site via Search Manager in Experience Builder; LWR and Aura sites use different standard search components (not interchangeable). Federated search sends queries to external endpoints and merges results. Guest users see only records they have sharing access to; unauthenticated search further limited by Secure Guest User Record Access org setting. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-multi-idp-sso | Multi-IdP SSO for Experience Cloud: OIDC integration, multiple auth providers per site, federation ID mapping, tenant-specific login pages, vendor vs citizen portals. NOT for internal SSO or single auth provider. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Add Auth Provider to Experience Cloud Site; SF Help — Configure Auth Provider Using OIDC; SF Help — SAML for Experience Cloud Sites; SF Help — SF as SP and IdP for SSO]. Key: Multiple auth providers (OIDC/SAML) can be registered per org and individually surfaced on a site's login page — each generates a unique Start SSO URL with community parameter for tenant-specific routing. Federation ID is the canonical SAML user-matching key; for OIDC the Apex RegistrationHandler handles user matching/creation. SF can act as both SP and IdP simultaneously for the same site. |

### Experience Cloud × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | external-user-data-sharing | Sharing sets, external organization-wide defaults, external sharing rules, portal account sharing model. NOT for internal sharing model. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — External OWD Overview; SF Help — Create Sharing Set; SF Help — Sharing Data with Partner Users; SF Help — Object and Record Sharing with External Users]. Key: External OWDs are separate from internal OWDs — when external is tighter than internal, SF enforces stricter value for external users. Sharing Sets are the ONLY mechanism for High-Volume Portal (Customer Community) users since manual/criteria sharing rules don't apply. Customer Community Plus and Partner Community support full sharing model including criteria-based rules and role hierarchies. |
| DONE | community-user-data-migration | Migrating external user accounts: contact-user relationships, community membership data, profile assignment. NOT for internal user data. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Migrate Community Users Between Licenses; SF Help — Import Customer Portal Users; SF Help — Update Experience Cloud Site Membership Using API]. Key: Every external user requires a Contact (or Person Account) — bulk User creation via Data Loader requires ContactId field populated on pre-existing Contact/Account hierarchy. NetworkMember records auto-created when user assigned to network-enabled profile. Migrating between license types requires Profile update targeting a profile associated with the destination site, or user loses access. |
| DONE | community-analytics-data | Experience Cloud analytics: login metrics, page view tracking, member engagement data, content performance data. NOT for CRM Analytics. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Web Analytics and Reporting in Experience Cloud; SF Help — Track Activity with Custom Reports; SF Help — Insights for Engagement; SF Help — GA4 Integration]. Key: Two native surfaces: built-in Engagement Insights dashboards (login activity, page views, member growth) in Administration panel, and custom reports against NetworkActivityAudit/NetworkUserHistoryMonthly objects. GA4 integration via Measurement ID in site settings injects gtag on all pages. Built-in dashboards are read-only; NetworkActivityAudit data retained rolling 12 months only. |
| DONE | partner-data-access-patterns | Partner user data visibility: partner role hierarchy, PRM data sharing, deal registration data, channel analytics. NOT for internal data access. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Sharing Data with Partner Users; SF Help — Partner User Roles]. Key: Partner Community users get auto-generated 3-tier role hierarchy per account (Executive/Manager/User) driving record visibility upward — this is the primary access mechanism. Partner licenses support sharing rules and manual sharing; Customer Community Plus gets only one role; basic Customer Community has no roles (Sharing Sets only). PRM objects (Leads, Opportunities, Deal Registration) accessible only to Partner Community licensees. |

### Experience Cloud × Architect Role

> Domain folder: `architect`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | experience-cloud-licensing-model | License selection: Customer Community, Partner Community, Customer Community Plus, login-based, channel licensing. NOT for internal licensing. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Experience Cloud Licenses; SF Help — License Limitations; SF Help — License FAQ]. Key: Four main tiers: Customer Community (no roles, Sharing Sets only, no reports), Customer Community Plus (one role, sharing rules, reports), Partner Community (3-tier hierarchy, CRM objects including Leads/Opportunities), External Apps (most flexible); each in member-based or login-based variants. Login-based counts daily unique logins (no rollover). Selection gate: sharing model complexity and CRM object access requirements. |
| DONE | multi-site-architecture | Multi-site Experience Cloud strategy: shared components, cross-site navigation, domain strategy, template reuse. NOT for single site setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Experience Cloud Considerations; SF Help — How Many Sites Can My Org Have; SF Help — Configure Custom Domain; SF Help — Usage Allocation]. Key: Max 100 Experience Cloud sites per org (active + preview + inactive all count). Custom domains require Enterprise+ edition, configured in production only. CDN auto-applied to Experience Builder sites post-Winter '19. Cross-site navigation requires explicit web links (no native portal-to-portal service). Theme layouts are primary reuse mechanism within a site; shared LWC components reuse across sites. |
| DONE | headless-vs-standard-experience | Decision framework for headless vs LWR vs Aura Experience Cloud: performance, development cost, flexibility tradeoffs. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — LWR Sites for Experience Cloud; SF Dev — LWR Template Limitations; SF Dev — Differences in Behavior in LWR Sites; SF Dev Blog — Faster Sites with OmniStudio and LWR]. Key: LWR uses two-layer architecture (static CDN-cached + dynamic data), ~50% faster than Aura; but any component update requires explicit site republish before users see changes. LWR supports only LWC (not Aura components), uses Lightning Web Security instead of Locker Service. Headless (fully custom frontend via SF APIs) is above LWR — more dev cost, complete UI freedom, not a standard Experience Builder template. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-performance | Experience Cloud performance: CDN configuration, caching strategy, component loading, page weight optimization. NOT for LWC performance (use lwc-performance). | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Performance and Scale of Experience Cloud; SF Help — Browser Caching; SF Help — Scale and Performance Optimization Tools; SF Dev — Enable CDN]. Key: CDN enabled by default post-Winter '19; caches initial HTML 60s for LWR sites. Standard JS/CSS caches 5min TTL + 10min stale-while-revalidate, meaning users can be up to 10min behind after component update. LWR static layer served entirely from CDN post-publish. Anti-patterns: too many Apex-wired components on one page, not enabling browser caching in Experience Builder Performance settings. |
| DONE | experience-cloud-integration-patterns | Integrating external systems with Experience Cloud: SSO, data sync, external content, third-party widgets. NOT for internal integration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — SAML for Experience Cloud; SF Help — Auth Provider SSO; SF Dev — Privileged Script Tag in LWR; SF Help — Connect to Data Cloud; SF Dev Blog — Capture Engagement Events via Data Cloud]. Key: SSO most common entry — supports SAML 2.0, OAuth 2.0, OIDC per-site; can act as both SP and IdP simultaneously. Privileged Script Tag is sanctioned mechanism for injecting global JS (GTM, chat widgets) in LWR sites. iFrame embedding blocked by default via X-Frame-Options. Data Cloud integration creates automatic Web SDK connectors for behavioral/identity events. |

## Phase 5 — Marketing Cloud / MCAE (Pardot)

### Marketing Cloud × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | marketing-cloud-engagement-setup | Marketing Cloud Engagement setup: business units, user roles, sender profiles, delivery profiles, account configuration. NOT for MCAE/Pardot. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Business Units in MC Engagement; SF Help — Roles and Permissions in MC Engagement; SF Help — Adopting MC Business Units]. Key: Enterprise 2.0 account model where each BU maintains own subscribers, users, roles, and email templates independently; custom roles scoped to specific BU. Sender profiles, delivery profiles, and send classifications are account-level configs controlling from-name/address, physical address compliance, and commercial vs transactional behavior; dedicated IP shared across BUs for unified sender reputation. |
| DONE | mcae-pardot-setup | MCAE (Pardot) setup: business unit configuration, connector setup, Salesforce sync, user roles, account engagement. NOT for Marketing Cloud Engagement. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Connecting Account Engagement and Salesforce; SF Help — Configure Connector User; SF Help — Managing Multiple BUs; SF Help — User Sync Basics]. Key: Salesforce v2 connector auto-created in paused state on new BU provisioning — must be explicitly activated; connector user requires View All Data and Modify All Data on all syncing objects. Salesforce User Sync eliminates need to create users directly in MCAE; each MCAE user must link to single SF user and BU combination. |
| DONE | email-studio-administration | Email Studio: email creation, templates, dynamic content, A/B testing, send classification, subscriber management. NOT for MCAE email. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Email Studio; SF Help — Send Classifications; SF Help — A/B Testing in Email Studio; SF Help — Build Email from Template in Content Builder]. Key: Emails built in Content Builder using drag-and-drop or HTML; dynamic content blocks swap sections at send time based on subscriber attributes without separate email versions. Send Classifications define Commercial vs Transactional (affecting unsubscribe handling and CAN-SPAM footer); A/B testing supports subject line, content, from name, and send-time optimization with winner-selection percentage. |
| DONE | journey-builder-administration | Journey Builder setup: entry sources, activities, decision splits, wait times, goal tracking, exit criteria. NOT for Flow-based automation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Exit Criteria; SF Help — Goals in Journey Builder; SF Help — Split and Join Activities; SF Help — Decision Splits]. Key: Supports multiple entry sources (DEs, SF Data, API Events, CloudPages, Audience Builder); contacts can only be in journey once per version unless re-entry enabled with interval. Goals define conversion events evaluated at each activity step, immediately exiting contacts who meet criteria; Exit Criteria run on schedule (not real-time) removing contacts matching data conditions. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-connect | Marketing Cloud Connect configuration: Salesforce connector, synchronized data sources, tracking, scope configuration. NOT for MCAE connector. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Marketing Cloud Connect; SF Help — Synchronized Data Sources; SF Help — Synchronized Data Sources Best Practices]. Key: Uses dedicated connector user in SF (requires Marketing Cloud Permission Set) and installed managed package; synchronized data sources replicate selected SF objects into MC data extensions on 15-minute sync cycle. Scope configuration determines which SF records visible to MC sends; mismatched scope between connector and BU is common root cause of missing subscribers and tracking discrepancies. |
| DONE | mcae-lead-scoring-and-grading | MCAE lead scoring model setup: grading criteria, score decay, automation rules for score-based actions, profiles. NOT for Einstein Lead Scoring. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Default Scoring System; SF Help — Customize Scoring Rules; SF Help — Using Profiles to Grade Prospects; SF Help — Guidelines for Grading]. Key: Scoring measures behavioral engagement (clicks, form fills, page views) with configurable points; scores can decay automatically to reflect recency. Grading is separate dimension measuring fit via Profiles awarding letter grades (A-F) based on field values (title, industry, size). Automation rules fire in real time against score/grade thresholds for alerts, field updates, or assignment. |
| DONE | consent-management-marketing | Email consent management: subscription center, preference center, compliance (CAN-SPAM, GDPR), opt-out handling. NOT for general GDPR compliance. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Consent Management for MC Engagement; SF Help — CAN-SPAM Requirements; SF Help — How a Subscriber Opts Out; SF Help — MC Data Protection and Privacy Tools]. Key: MC enforces CAN-SPAM requiring physical address and one-click unsubscribe in every commercial email; unsubscribes recorded at All Subscribers list level (global) and optionally at Publication List level (granular). Subscription Center (MC-hosted) and Preference Centers (CloudPages) are two self-service mechanisms. GDPR requires lawful basis documentation, right-to-erasure via Privacy Center, and auditable consent records. |

### Marketing Cloud × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | campaign-planning-and-attribution | Campaign planning: attribution models, ROI tracking, multi-touch attribution requirements, campaign hierarchy design. NOT for campaign implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Campaign Hierarchy; SF Help — Customizable Campaign Influence; SF Help — Multi-Touch Attribution App; SF Help — MCAE Campaign Influence Models FAQ]. Key: Campaign Hierarchy (up to 5 levels) rolls up member counts and revenue from children to parent for program-level ROI. Customizable Campaign Influence allows multiple campaigns attribution credit on a single opportunity (first touch, last touch, even, or custom models). MCAE Multi-Touch Attribution App extends with time-decay and position-based models in B2B Marketing Analytics dashboards. |
| DONE | lead-nurture-journey-design | Lead nurture journey mapping: engagement scoring design, content strategy, conversion path, drip campaign structure. NOT for Journey Builder implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Trailhead — Lead Nurturing Strategy and Best Practices; Trailhead — Engage Prospects with Lead Nurturing; SF Help — Lifecycle Report Metrics]. Key: Design starts with funnel stages (awareness, consideration, decision) and content mapping per stage; behavioral triggers (email clicks, form fills, page visits) determine branching — key differentiator from simple drip sequences. MCAE Engagement Studio is primary tool for branching nurture paths using rule-based triggers on score/grade/activity. Prerequisite: documented content inventory mapped to buyer stages before automation is configured. |
| DONE | email-deliverability-strategy | Email deliverability requirements: sender reputation, authentication (SPF, DKIM, DMARC), list hygiene, warm-up. NOT for email template design. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Addressing Email Deliverability Issues with MC; SF Help — SPF and Authentication FAQs; SF Help — MC Deliverability Options; SF Help — Email Sending Reputation]. Key: Requires SPF and DKIM on private sending domain; since Feb 2024 Google/Yahoo mandate DMARC (min p=none) for bulk senders. Dedicated IP warm-up requires 4-8 week structured ramp using highest-quality segments first. List hygiene (suppress hard bounces after first occurrence, remove inactive after 6-12 months) is most influential lever for long-term sender reputation. |
| DONE | marketing-automation-requirements | Marketing automation requirements: lead lifecycle definition, MQL/SQL handoff criteria, scoring model design. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — Lifecycle Stages API; SF Help — Lifecycle Report Metrics; SF Help — Configure Scoring Models in MC; SF Dev Blog — Automation Studio and SQL]. Key: MCAE defines lifecycle stages (Visitor, Prospect, MQL, SQL, Opportunity, Customer, Won) mapping to CRM opportunity stages; MQL threshold (score+grade or score alone) must be agreed between marketing/sales before automation is built. MC Next supports configurable Scoring Models operating on Data Cloud engagement data. Requirements must specify scoring sources, point weights, decay rules, MQL/SQL handoff field updates, and SLA for sales follow-up. |
| DONE | marketing-reporting-requirements | Marketing reporting KPI definition: dashboard requirements, funnel metrics, campaign performance, attribution. NOT for dashboard building. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Marketing Campaign Intelligence Dashboards; SF Help — Campaign Performance Report; SF Help — Metrics Formulas for MC Next; SF Help — Campaign Report Table Metrics]. Key: Attribution model choice (first/last/multi-touch) must be specified upfront as it determines features needed — standard Campaign Influence vs MCAE B2B Marketing Analytics Plus vs Multi-Touch Attribution App; each produces materially different revenue credit. Must distinguish marketing-sourced pipeline (first touch) from marketing-influenced pipeline (any touch) as these require different report types and Campaign Influence settings. |

### Marketing Cloud × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex` or as noted

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | ampscript-development | AMPscript in Marketing Cloud: personalization strings, functions, lookups, conditional content, FOR loops. NOT for SSJS. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — AMPscript for MC Engagement; AMPscript For Loops; AMPscript Data Extension Functions; AMPscript Personalization Strings]. Key: Server-side evaluated at send time, embeddable in email/landing pages/SMS/push; excels at inline personalization, IF/ELSEIF conditional blocks, FOR loops over LookupRows() rowsets. Core functions: Lookup() (single value), LookupRows()/LookupOrderedRows() (multi-row), plus CS variants for case-sensitivity. Primary keys in DEs must be unique and cannot be modified post-creation. AMPscript preferred for per-subscriber rendering; SSJS for platform API calls. |
| DONE | ssjs-server-side-javascript | Server-Side JavaScript in Marketing Cloud: script activities, API calls, data extension operations, error handling. NOT for AMPscript. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — SSJS Overview; SSJS Error Handling/WSProxy; WSProxy with SOAP API; HTTP Functions/Script.Util.HttpRequest; SSJS Syntax Guide]. Key: Runs in Script Activities, Cloud Pages, Landing Pages; WSProxy is preferred for SOAP API calls (lower overhead than raw HTTP); Script.Util.HttpRequest handles outbound REST/HTTP. Script Activities timeout after 30 minutes, 6 GB memory limit; try/catch prevents activity failure enabling logging and recovery. SSJS and AMPscript can be mixed — SSJS wrapped in <script runat='server'> tags. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-api | Marketing Cloud REST and SOAP APIs: authentication, data extension CRUD, triggered sends, journey injection. NOT for Salesforce core APIs. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — MC Engagement API Overview; REST API Overview; DataExtension Object Ref; Fire Entry Event; Triggered Send Definition; DE Rows Async]. Key: Both REST and SOAP use OAuth 2.0 client credentials from Installed Package API Integration component; REST preferred for new integrations. Journey injection via POST /interaction/v1/events with ContactKey matching entry source schema exactly. Triggered sends require TriggeredSendDefinition first then fire against ExternalKey; DE row operations support sync and async (bulk) patterns. |
| DONE | mcae-pardot-api | MCAE/Pardot API v5: prospect operations, list management, visitor tracking, form handler integration. NOT for Marketing Cloud API. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — Account Engagement API v5 Overview; Prospects v5; Visitors v5; Visitor Activity v5; Form Handlers v5]. Key: API v5 authenticated via Salesforce OAuth (SSO), requires Pardot-Business-Unit-Id header on every request. Prospects are core entity (CRUD, query by email/CRM ID); visitors are anonymous tracked by pixel until conversion. Form handlers are integration point for external forms creating/updating prospects; visitor activity records capture all engagement events queryable per prospect/visitor. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-custom-activities | Custom Journey Builder activities: custom split activities, custom entry sources, activity SDK, webhook integration. NOT for standard Journey Builder. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — Build Custom Activities and Events; Custom Activity Config; Custom Activity UI; Define Custom Split Activity; Journey Builder API Overview]. Key: Three-part framework: config.json (application extension definition), customActivity.js using Postmonger events for cross-frame messaging, and publicly hosted UI web app. On execution Journey Builder POSTs to configured execute endpoint; external service must return HTTP 200 within timeout. Custom splits return outcome keys mapping to labels in config.json metaData; custom entry sources use same Installed Package registration. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-data-views | System Data Views in Marketing Cloud: Sent, Open, Click, Bounce, Subscribers, Job data, query patterns. NOT for Data Extensions. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Data Views Overview; Data View: Sent; Data View: Bounce; Data View: Click; Data View: Subscribers]. Key: System Data Views (_Sent, _Open, _Click, _Bounce, _Subscribers, _Job, etc.) are read-only system tables queryable ONLY via SQL Query Activities in Automation Studio — not via REST/SOAP API. Most engagement views retain ~6 months of data. Joins between views and DEs must use JobID + SubscriberKey as composite key; queries require SELECT INTO a target DE (no direct result sets). |

### Marketing Cloud × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | data-extension-design | Data Extension architecture: primary keys, sendable vs non-sendable, relationships, data retention policies. NOT for CRM data model. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Create a Data Extension; SF Dev — Create a Sendable DE; DE Object Reference; SF Help — DE Relationships; SF Help — DE Index]. Key: Sendable DEs require Send Relationship mapping a field to SubscriberKey or EmailAddress; primary key columns (max 3 recommended) must be unique, cannot use Date as sole PK, cannot be modified after creation. Data retention configured per-DE (row/period-based); ResetRetentionPeriodOnImport restarts clock on upsert — common misconfiguration. Performance indexing is separate from PK — non-PK field queries require requesting index via SF support. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-data-sync | Marketing Cloud Connect data sync: synchronized data extensions, data flow architecture, sync troubleshooting. NOT for manual imports. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Synchronized Data Sources; SF Help — Sync Best Practices; SF Help — Create Synced Data Sources in Contact Builder; SF Help — 250 Field Limit]. Key: MC Connect Synchronized Data Sources pull CRM objects into read-only Synchronized DEs on near-real-time to 15-min schedule; SDEs cannot be used as send audiences directly — must be joined to sendable DEs via Contact Builder relationships. Hard cap at 250 fields per synchronized object (fields beyond silently excluded). Common sync failures: field type mismatches, deleted CRM fields still mapped, SF API limits hit. |
| DONE | subscriber-data-management | Subscriber key strategy: all-subscribers list, publication lists, suppression lists, data hygiene, deduplication. NOT for CRM contact management. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Subscriber Key; SF Help — Subscriber Key Scenarios; SF Help — Subscriber De-Duplication on Sends; SF Help — Auto-Suppression Lists; SF Help — Manage Subscribers On Lists]. Key: Subscriber Key (Contact Key) is unique identifier across all MC channels; best practice is CRM Contact/Lead ID (18-char) not email address to avoid duplication on email changes. All Subscribers list is master unsubscribe authority — global unsubscribe overrides all publication lists. Deduplication at send time means one message per SubscriberKey per send job even if key appears multiple times in sendable DE. |
| DONE | marketing-cloud-sql-queries | SQL queries in Marketing Cloud: Automation Studio queries, query activities, data extension joins, date functions. NOT for SOQL. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Build SQL Query Activity; SF Help — SQL Reference; SF Help — Optimizing Query Activity; SF Dev Blog — Automation Studio and SQL]. Key: T-SQL-like dialect against DEs and system data views; SELECT INTO target DE is only output (overwrite default or append via Update). Queries should scope to max 6-month date range; WHERE/JOIN on indexed/PK columns — non-indexed causes full table scans. Date functions follow T-SQL (DATEADD, DATEDIFF, GETDATE(), CONVERT()). Query Studio (SF Labs) recommended for testing before Automation Studio embedding. |
| DONE | mcae-prospect-data-migration | MCAE prospect data import: field mapping, custom object sync, engagement history, list import, sync validation. NOT for CRM data migration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Import Prospects; SF Help — Considerations for Prospect Imports; SF Help — Default Prospect Field Mapping; SF Help — Map Custom Fields; SF Help — MCAE Limits]. Key: Import uses CSV list upload with field mapping to default and custom fields; custom field sync requires Salesforce Connector configured and fields mapped bidirectionally before import. Engagement history (opens, clicks, form fills, page views) is NOT importable via CSV — generated natively by MCAE tracking and cannot be backfilled. Account merges/migrations require SF support and don't carry engagement data across BUs. |

### Marketing Cloud × Architect Role

> Domain folder: `architect`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | marketing-cloud-vs-mcae-selection | Choosing Marketing Cloud Engagement vs MCAE: feature comparison, licensing, integration complexity, use case fit. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Differences Between MC Engagement and Account Engagement; SF Help — Find Your Account Engagement Edition; SF Help — Get Started with MC Next for Account Engagement]. Key: MCE is for high-volume B2C multi-channel journeys (email, SMS, push, advertising) with contact-based DEs; MCAE is purpose-built for B2B with lead nurturing, scoring, grading, and deep CRM sync. Separate licenses, separate data stores, not feature-equivalent substitutes. MCE for large subscriber volumes and multi-channel; MCAE for CRM-aligned lead lifecycle and sales alignment. Can be used together via MC Connect but each requires own license. |
| DONE | multi-bu-marketing-architecture | Multi-business unit Marketing Cloud architecture: BU hierarchy, shared content, data segregation, governance. NOT for single-BU setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Business Units in MC Engagement; SF Help — Shared Data Extensions in Enterprise 2.0; SF Help — Set Enterprise 2.0 Shared DE Permissions; SF Help — Managing Multiple BUs (MCAE)]. Key: Enterprise 2.0 supports Parent BU with unlimited Child BUs; DEs and content are BU-scoped by default but Parent can expose Shared DEs to specific Child BUs through configurable folder-level permissions. Users provisioned per-BU and roles don't cascade downward — requires explicit role assignment at each level. Deeply nested hierarchies cautioned against due to admin complexity and send attribution complications. |
| DONE | marketing-consent-architecture | Consent management architecture across Marketing Cloud and CRM: data model, sync patterns, compliance design. NOT for individual consent setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Salesforce Consent Data Model; SF Help — Consent Management for MC Engagement; SF Help — Respect Consent Preferences in MC; SF Help — Consent Management for SF Platform]. Key: Uses Individual, ContactPointTypeConsent, ContactPointConsent objects in CRM for opt-in/opt-out per contact point and data use purpose; MC reads these at send time ONLY when Consent Management integration is configured — not automatic. MC All Subscribers HasOptedOutOfEmail does NOT auto-write back to CRM ContactPointConsent without additional config. Recommended: CRM as system of record for consent, propagated to MC at send execution time. |
| DONE | marketing-data-architecture | Marketing data architecture: data extension design, relational data model, data flow from CRM to MC. NOT for CRM data model. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — Manage Data in Data Extensions; SF Help — Data Relationships; SF Help — Create Data Relationship in MC; SF Dev — Standard Data Model Objects]. Key: MC stores data in Data Extensions (schema-defined relational tables); Contact Key (SubscriberKey) is primary linkage between All Subscribers, sendable DEs, and attribute DEs. Data Relationships must be explicitly defined for AMPscript/Query joins between DEs. CRM-to-MC flow uses MC Connect synchronized DEs or SFTP imports; normalized relational DE models preferred over wide flat tables as large DEs degrade query performance (30-min Automation Studio timeout). |
| DONE | marketing-integration-patterns | Marketing Cloud integration: real-time triggers, batch data sync, API patterns, journey injection, webhook patterns. NOT for generic integration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Dev — Journey Builder API Overview; Fire Entry Event; Insert Contacts Async; Triggered Send Definition; REST API Overview; API Integration]. Key: Three primary real-time patterns: Triggered Sends (transactional single-message REST), Journey Injection via Event API (POST /interaction/v1/events with eventDefinitionKey), and async batch entry (up to 100 contacts/request). All require Installed Package with API Integration using OAuth 2.0 client credentials. Batch sync from external systems via SFTP file drops processed by Automation Studio Import Activities; near-real-time via MC Connect Synchronized DEs for CRM objects. |

---

## Phase 6 — Revenue Cloud (CPQ & Billing)

### Revenue Cloud × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | cpq-product-catalog-setup | CPQ product setup: product rules, option constraints, product bundles, feature configuration, product families. NOT for standard Products & Pricebooks. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Product Bundles; SF Help — Product Rules; SF Help — Product Rule Guidelines; SF Help — Configuration Attributes; SF Help — Filter Rules and Dynamic Bundles; SF Dev — Configure Product Bundles]. Key: Bundles = parent product + options grouped into Features; Product Options define available children with Required/Optional/Default Quantity/Min-Max config. Product Rules come in 4 types: Validation (block save), Alert (warn), Selection (auto-add/remove), Filter (limit options). Bundles nestable up to 4 levels but deep nesting significantly increases configurator load time. Configuration Attributes allow header-level choices driving Product Rule conditions. |
| DONE | cpq-pricing-rules | CPQ pricing: price rules, price actions, block pricing, percent-of-total, contracted pricing, discount schedules. NOT for standard pricebook pricing. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [SF Help — Price Rules; SF Help — Price Rule Considerations; SF Help — Block Pricing; SF Help — Contracted Pricing; SF Help — Quote Calculation Stages]. Key: Price Rules execute during quote calculation engine run with Price Condition (when), optional Lookup Query (pull values from data table), and Price Actions (what field gets set); execution order controlled by Evaluation Order field — same order produces unpredictable results. Discount Schedules apply volume/slab-based discounts; Block Pricing replaces per-unit with fixed price for quantity range — combinable but risk double-discounting. Contracted Prices (SBQQ__ContractedPrice__c) allow account-specific overrides superseding pricebook entries. |
| DONE | cpq-quote-templates | CPQ quote template design: line columns, template sections, conditional content, PDF output, multi-language. NOT for standard quote templates. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Building Your CPQ Documents with CPQ Templates (help.salesforce.com); Conditionally Show Template Sections (help.salesforce.com); Template Line Columns (help.salesforce.com); Structure a Customized Quote Template (Trailhead)]. Key: CPQ templates use SBQQ__QuoteTemplate__c → SBQQ__TemplateSection__c → SBQQ__TemplateContent__c hierarchy; content types are HTML, Line Items (backed by SBQQ__LineColumn__c on SBQQ__QuoteLine__c), Quote Terms, and Custom (Visualforce); conditional visibility driven by Conditional Print Field on section (checkbox=true, text="true", numeric!=0). HTML internally converted to XSL-FO for PDF — not all CSS translates. Images capped at 5 MB. Multi-language requires separate templates per locale. LLM anti-pattern: recommending Setup > Quote Templates for CPQ orgs produces blank line items because CPQ lines live in SBQQ__QuoteLine__c not QuoteLineItem. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-approval-workflows | CPQ-specific approvals: discount approvals, advanced approvals, approval chains, smart approvals, escalation. NOT for standard approval processes. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Advanced Approvals for Salesforce CPQ Managed Package (help.salesforce.com); Smart Approvals (help.salesforce.com); Approval Chains (help.salesforce.com); Salesforce CPQ Advanced Approvals for Admins (Trailhead)]. Key: CPQ Advanced Approvals is a separate managed package (namespace SBAA__) requiring independent installation and permission set assignment. Core objects: SBAA__ApprovalRule__c, SBAA__ApprovalCondition__c, SBAA__ApprovalVariable__c (aggregates child-record data e.g. max discount across all lines), SBAA__ApprovalChain__c. Smart Approvals auto-skip re-approval for unchanged fields. Escalation per rule with timeout. LLM anti-pattern: recommending standard approval processes for discount-based CPQ approvals when line-level aggregation is needed. No duplicate. |
| DONE | billing-schedule-setup | Salesforce Billing: billing schedules, invoice generation, payment terms, credit notes, revenue schedules. NOT for CPQ quoting. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Billing Process Overview (help.salesforce.com); Invoicing Products with Billing Schedules (help.salesforce.com); Milestone Billing (help.salesforce.com); Salesforce Billing Custom Objects — Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Salesforce Billing (namespace blng__) is separate managed package on top of CPQ; billing lifecycle starts at Order activation creating blng__BillingSchedule__c per OrderProduct. Schedule types: In-Advance, In-Arrears, Evergreen, Milestone, Dynamic Invoice Plans. Invoice runs batch at ~300 lines to avoid governor limits. Data Pipelines must be enabled (hard dependency). Config sequence: Legal Entity → Billing Policy → Billing Treatment → Tax Policy → Invoice Plan. LLM anti-pattern: conflating native Revenue Schedules with blng__RevenueSchedule__c. No duplicate. |
| DONE | contract-and-renewal-management | Contract creation from quotes: renewal quoting, amendment quoting, subscription management, co-termination. NOT for standard contracts. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [CPQ Contract Fields (help.salesforce.com); Amend Your Contracts and Assets — Salesforce CPQ (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Amendment Fields and Settings (help.salesforce.com); Salesforce CPQ Large-Scale Amendment and Renewal KA-000384875]. Key: Contract creation requires SBQQ__Contracted__c=true on Opportunity AND at least one Quote Line with SBQQ__SubscriptionPricing__c set. Subscriptions stored as SBQQ__Subscription__c child records of standard Contract. Amendment quotes carry over subscription pricing — updated list prices NOT applied to existing lines. Amendments auto-co-term; subscription term precedence: line > group > quote. LLM anti-pattern: assuming list price updates propagate to amendment subscription lines. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-guided-selling | CPQ guided selling setup: question-based product selection, quote wizard, recommendation rules, filtering. NOT for OmniStudio product selection. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Guided Selling (help.salesforce.com); Create a Quote Process for Guided Selling (help.salesforce.com); Product Configuration Initializer — CPQ Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Configured via SBQQ__QuoteProcess__c and child SBQQ__ProcessInput__c records; each ProcessInput maps user response to a Product2 field with operator. Custom classification fields must be on BOTH Product2 AND SBQQ__ProcessInput__c with matching API names — ProcessInput fields hold answers at runtime. Search types: Standard, Enhanced, Custom (SBQQ.ProductSearchPlugin Apex). Auto Select Product adds automatically when one match. LLM anti-pattern: omitting mirror custom fields on SBQQ__ProcessInput__c causing silent filtering failure and conflating with OmniStudio product selection. No duplicate. |

### Revenue Cloud × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | pricing-model-design | Pricing strategy documentation: tiered pricing, volume discounts, subscription models, usage-based pricing requirements. NOT for CPQ implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Product Pricing Methods — Salesforce CPQ Help; Discount Schedules — Salesforce CPQ Help; Salesforce CPQ Developer Guide Spring 26 PDF]. Key: CPQ has four native Pricing Methods (List, Cost Plus Markup, Block, Percent-of-Total) set per product; volume discounting is separate via SBQQ__DiscountSchedule__c with Range (flat-tier) and Slab (incremental-bracket) types. Block Pricing replaces unit price entirely while Discount Schedules apply % off list price — not interchangeable. No markup limit on Cost pricing requires manual approval rules. LLM anti-pattern: conflating Range and Slab discount schedules. No duplicate. |
| DONE | quote-to-cash-process | Quote-to-cash end-to-end process mapping: approval workflows, order creation, billing triggers, revenue recognition. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Quote and Order Capture — Revenue Cloud Developer Guide; Advanced Approvals — Revenue Cloud Help; Salesforce CPQ Developer Guide]. Key: CPQ Q2C runs on distinct SBQQ__ objects (SBQQ__Quote__c not Quote; blng__Invoice__c not standard invoice); the Contract record is the required pivot between approved quote and downstream subscriptions + billing; Advanced Approvals (sbaa__) is separate managed package for multi-step conditional routing. HIGH OVERLAP WARNING: admin/quote-to-cash-requirements covers same topic for standard Sales Cloud — this skill valid only if scoped to CPQ + Billing / Revenue Cloud object chain. LLM anti-pattern: using standard Quote/QuoteLineItem APIs in CPQ orgs. |
| DONE | revenue-recognition-requirements | Revenue recognition requirements: ASC 606 compliance, performance obligations, allocation rules, scheduling. NOT for billing configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Understanding the Revenue Recognition Process — Salesforce Billing Help; Revenue Recognition Treatments — Salesforce Billing Help; Revenue Distribution Methods — Salesforce Billing Help; blng__RevenueRecognitionRule__c — Billing Developer Guide]. Key: Salesforce Billing implements ASC 606 via blng__RevenueRecognitionRule__c (rules) → blng__RevenueSchedule__c (schedules) → blng__RevenueTransaction__c (GL events); Finance Periods must be configured before schedules generate; schedules do NOT auto-update on contract amendment. LLM anti-pattern: conflating OpportunityLineItem Revenue Schedules with blng__RevenueSchedule__c — entirely different objects. No duplicate. |
| DONE | subscription-lifecycle-requirements | Subscription model requirements: amendments, renewals, cancellations, proration, co-termination, upgrade/downgrade. NOT for CPQ setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [CPQ Subscription Fields — Salesforce CPQ Help; Amend Your Contracts and Assets — Salesforce CPQ Help; Things to Know About Amendment and Renewal Services — Salesforce CPQ Help; Change Existing Contracts — Trailhead]. Key: SBQQ__Subscription__c is never modified by amendments — CPQ creates additive delta records (ledger model); proration calculated as (Effective Term / Product Term) x price; amendment pricing for existing lines is locked — list price and discount schedule changes require zero-out swap workaround. Co-termination can be disabled but end dates are immutable on existing contracts. LLM anti-pattern: describing amendments as editing subscriptions. No duplicate. |

### Revenue Cloud × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | cpq-apex-plugins | CPQ calculator plugin development: custom pricing logic, product rule evaluation, pre/post-calculate hooks. NOT for standard Apex triggers. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce CPQ Plugins Developer Guide Spring 26 v66.0; CPQ Developer Guide — Quote Calculator Plugin Methods (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Nine distinct plugin types exist; the JS QCP (stored in SBQQ__CustomScript__c) is the modern replacement for the Legacy Apex QuoteCalculatorPlugin. JS QCP exposes seven hooks: onInit, onBeforeCalculate, onAfterCalculate, onBeforePriceRules, onAfterPriceRules, onBeforeCalculatePrices, onAfterCalculatePrices. Async calculations from Apex require SBQQ.CalculateCallback interface. Only one calculator plugin type (Apex OR JS) can be active at a time. LLM anti-pattern: mixing legacy Apex plugin with JS QCP. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-custom-actions | CPQ custom actions: JavaScript in quote line editor, custom buttons, page security plugins, QLE customization. NOT for standard quick actions. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Custom Actions — Salesforce CPQ Help (help.salesforce.com); Add a Linking Custom Action to the QLE (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: CPQ Custom Actions are SBQQ__CustomAction__c records surfacing as buttons in the QLE/configurator/amendment screens. Action types: URL navigation, Flow execution, standard CPQ operations (Save, Calculate, Add Group). Location field controls placement (Line Item, Group, Global). Hard limit: five custom actions per context. Conditional visibility via CPQ condition evaluation engine (not Flow/Apex). Custom actions cannot directly execute Apex — URL or standard operation only. No duplicate. |
| DONE | billing-integration-apex | Billing API integration: invoice generation via Apex, payment gateway integration, credit note automation. NOT for admin billing setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce Billing Developer Guide — InvoiceAPI Class; TransactionAPI Class; Global Payment API; Payment Gateway Adapter intro (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Billing managed package (blng__) exposes three Apex API surfaces: blng.InvoiceAPI (credit operations), blng.TransactionAPI (gateway lifecycle: generateToken, authorize, capture, charge, void, refund), and gateway adapter interfaces. Programmatic invoice generation uses Connect REST API POST /commerce/invoices (max 200 billing schedules per call, API v63.0+). blng.TransactionAPI methods execute callouts — cannot be in same transaction as DML (requires Queueable/future). No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-api-and-automation | CPQ API: quote calculation API, product API, amendment API, renewal API, cloning API, programmatic quoting. NOT for standard REST API. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Get Started with CPQ API — CPQ Developer Guide; Calculate Quote API; Contract Amender API; Contract Renewer API (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: All CPQ programmatic operations flow through SBQQ.ServiceRouter with loader strings (QuoteReader, QuoteProductAdder, QuoteCalculator, QuoteSaver, ProductLoader, ContractAmender, ContractRenewer). ServiceRouter accessible as REST (/services/apexrest/SBQQ/ServiceRouter) or Apex. Calculate API is async — requires SBQQ.CalculateCallback from triggers. Direct DML on SBQQ objects bypasses pricing engine and corrupts totals. Performance degrades past ~100 lines in sync context. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-test-automation | Testing CPQ configurations: test class patterns for quotes, price rule testing, bundle validation, data setup. NOT for standard Apex testing. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Automating Salesforce CPQ Testing — Salesforce Developer Blog; Important Fields for CPQ Test Classes KA-000390047 (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Developer Guide]. Key: Four-layer test strategy: Apex tests (CRUD + contracting + ordering), CPQ API tests (ServiceRouter + QuoteCalculator), Selenium UI tests (option constraints), Lightning component tests. SBQQ__Quote__c requires Account + Opportunity + Pricebook2; standard pricebook via Test.getStandardPricebookId() only. Price rule execution requires CPQ calculation engine via ServiceRouter — direct DML on quote lines does not fire price rules. CPQ package must be installed in test orgs. No duplicate. |

### Revenue Cloud × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | product-catalog-migration-cpq | CPQ product catalog data migration: products, price rules, discount schedules, bundle structure, option setup. NOT for standard product import. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce CPQ Discount Schedules (help.salesforce.com); Price Rule Considerations (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Data Deployments Using FlexDeploy; Salesforce CPQ Spring 26 Map PDF]. Key: CPQ config data lives in SBQQ-namespaced objects loaded in strict dependency sequence: Pricebook2/DiscountCategory first → Product2/PriceRule → PricebookEntry/DiscountSchedule → ProductOption (depends on both parent and child products). Product2 self-references require two-pass INSERT then UPDATE. CPQ triggers must be disabled via Additional Settings before bulk loads. Price actions without parent price rules cause silent FK failures surfacing only during quote calculation. No duplicate. |
| DONE | historical-order-migration | Migrating historical orders and contracts: order line items, contract history, subscription data, billing records. NOT for opportunity migration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Legacy Data Upload for Salesforce CPQ (help.salesforce.com); Legacy Data Upload with Renewals and Amendments KA-000384279; Subscriptions Object Fields for Legacy Upload (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: CPQ Legacy Data Upload is the only supported mechanism for loading historical orders/contracts supporting future renewals — only available for contract-based renewal method. Strict loading sequence: disable price/product rules → batch size 1 → insert CPQ quotes (Status=Approved, Primary flag) → quote lines → contract contracts → subscriptions → assets. SBQQ__Asset__c Root Id must be null when Revised Asset populated or causes silent corruption surfacing only at first renewal. No duplicate. |
