| DONE | cpq-data-model | CPQ data model understanding: Quote, QuoteLine, Product, PriceRule, Subscription objects and relationships. NOT for standard data model. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [CPQ Object Relationships — Salesforce CPQ Help; CPQ Quote/QuoteLine/Subscription Fields — Salesforce CPQ Help; CPQ API QuoteModel/QuoteLineModel — Developer Guide]. Key: CPQ installs parallel SBQQ__ object graph — SBQQ__Quote__c / SBQQ__QuoteLine__c / SBQQ__QuoteLineGroup__c / SBQQ__DiscountSchedule__c / SBQQ__PriceRule__c / SBQQ__Subscription__c — none are standard Quote/QuoteLineItem. Direct DML on CPQ-managed fields bypasses pricing logic — must use CPQ Quote API (QuoteModel/QuoteLineModel). Partial overlap with architect/cpq-vs-standard-products-decision (object confusion anti-pattern) but no skill documents full SBQQ__ graph. No duplicate. |
| DONE | billing-data-reconciliation | Billing data reconciliation: invoice-to-payment matching, revenue recognition data, financial reporting alignment. NOT for CRM reporting. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Invoice-Based Revenue Recognition Reporting (help.salesforce.com); Understanding Revenue Recognition Process (help.salesforce.com); Billing Invoice Data Model — Revenue Cloud Data Model Gallery (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Reconciliation chain runs SBQQ__QuoteLine__c → OrderItem → blng__BillingSchedule__c → blng__Invoice__c → blng__InvoiceLine__c → blng__Payment__c. Invoice-to-payment matching via blng__PaymentAllocation__c; unallocated partial payments do not auto-close invoices. Revenue recognition governed by blng__RevenueRecognitionRule__c per product — missing rules produce silent /bin/zsh revenue entries. Revenue Transaction Error Log object is first-look diagnostic. No duplicate. |

### Revenue Cloud × Architect Role

> Domain folder: `architect`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | cpq-architecture-patterns | CPQ solution architecture: bundle design, pricing engine performance, multi-currency CPQ, integration strategy. NOT for individual feature design. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [CPQ Quote Calculation Sequence (help.salesforce.com); Guidelines for Multi-Currency CPQ (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Configuration API (developer.salesforce.com); CPQ Object Relationships (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: QLE cannot reliably save quotes beyond 200-300 line items; pricing waterfall is fixed: List → Contracted → Block → Discount Schedules → Price Rules → Net. QCP (JS escape hatch) has 131,072 char limit on SBQQ_Code__c forcing static resource architecture for large plugins. Multi-currency stores all pricing in corporate currency; dated exchange rates not natively supported. External systems must use /SBQQ/ServiceRouter REST API not direct DML. No duplicate. |
| DUPLICATE | cpq-vs-industries-cpq | Deciding between Salesforce CPQ and Industries CPQ (Vlocity): feature comparison, industry fit, migration paths. NOT for implementation. | Covered by skills/omnistudio/industries-cpq-vs-salesforce-cpq (comprehensive feature comparison, decision criteria, migration paths already documented) |
| DONE | cpq-performance-optimization | CPQ performance: quote calculation speed, large bundles, plugin optimization, caching strategies, batch calculations. NOT for generic Apex performance. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Large Quote Performance Settings (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Quote Calculation Stages (help.salesforce.com); Javascript Quote Calculator Plugin (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Large Quote Mode is primary lever — enables async server-side calculation past configurable line threshold; practical limit 200-300 lines before governor pressure. QCP fields declaration is mandatory for performance — undeclared fields cause silent null reads; overdeclaring inflates payload. SBQQ_Code__c capped at 131,072 chars forcing static resource + eval() architecture for large plugins. Calculate Quote API not a performance substitute — runs at async speed. LLM anti-pattern: enabling Large Quote mode without communicating UX change to users. No duplicate. |
| DONE | cpq-integration-with-erp | CPQ to ERP integration: order sync, pricing sync, inventory check, configuration validation, error handling. NOT for generic integration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [MuleSoft Accelerator for SAP — Quote-to-Cash; Pricing and Calculation Package Settings (help.salesforce.com); Get Started with Salesforce CPQ API (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Order activation status (not quote close) is canonical ERP trigger point. ERP should be pricing master fetched at CPQ calculation time — maintaining full copy of ERP pricing in CPQ price books causes drift. Inventory checks must be non-blocking (no callouts from QCP plugin execution context). Amendment orders are delta quantities not net-new ERP orders. CPQ quote lines live on SBQQ__QuoteLine__c not QuoteLineItem — ERP integrations querying wrong object get empty results. Additive to architect/sales-cloud-integration-patterns. No duplicate. |
| DONE | subscription-management-architecture | Subscription lifecycle architecture: amendment flow, renewal automation, co-termination design, billing integration. NOT for billing setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Amend Your Contracts and Assets — Salesforce CPQ (help.salesforce.com); CPQ Amendment Fields and Settings; Subscription and Renewal Package Settings; Large-Scale Amendment and Renewal KA-000384875]. Key: CPQ uses ledger model — amendments create new SBQQ__Subscription__c delta records never modifying existing ones. Price changes require swap pattern (zero existing + add new line). Preserve Bundle Structure must be checked for bundle amendments but silently ignored when Combine Subscription Quantities active. Two service modes: Legacy (sync) and Large-Scale (async batch) with different field behavior. Co-termination Start Date is most sensitive field — post-sale edits break proration. No duplicate. |

---

## Phase 7 — Field Service (FSL)

### FSL × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsl-work-order-management | Work Order configuration: work types, work order line items, service appointments, status flow, auto-creation. NOT for case management. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Guidelines for Creating Work Orders (help.salesforce.com); Create Work Types (help.salesforce.com); WorkOrder — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Track Field Service Jobs (Trailhead)]. Key: Core model is WorkOrder → WorkOrderLineItem → ServiceAppointment → AssignedResource. WorkType template stores Estimated Duration and auto-creates ServiceAppointment when AutoCreateSvcAppt enabled. Critical: Work Order status and Service Appointment status are completely independent — no built-in cascade. Maintenance Plans auto-generate WOs 3x daily. Limits: 10,000 child records per WO; 500 WOLI in Gantt. LLM anti-pattern: assuming WO and SA statuses are linked/cascading. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-service-territory-setup | Service territory setup: territory types, operating hours, territory members, territory hierarchy, polygons. NOT for ETM territories. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Guidelines for Creating Service Territories (help.salesforce.com); Set Up Service Territories Operating Hours and Shifts (help.salesforce.com); ServiceTerritory Object Reference (developer.salesforce.com); Field Service Core Data Model]. Key: ServiceTerritory + ServiceTerritoryMember (junction to ServiceResource) + OperatingHours/TimeSlot. Member types: Primary (one active per resource), Secondary (multiple, for occasional work), Relocation (temporary, requires start/end dates — routing engine skips travel calculation between primary and relocation boundaries). Hard Boundary work rule only honors Primary/Relocation not Secondary. Limits: 50 resources/territory; 1,000 SA/day/territory. LLM anti-pattern: conflating FSL ServiceTerritory with Sales Cloud Territory2/ETM. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-resource-management | Service resource setup: skills, capacity, availability, preferred resources, resource types, certification. NOT for user management. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Guidelines for Creating Service Resources (help.salesforce.com); Define Capacity-Based Resources (help.salesforce.com); ServiceResourceSkill — Field Service Developer Guide; Field Service Limits]. Key: ServiceResource (types: Technician, Crew) links to User or can be non-user for vehicles/tools. Skills via ServiceResourceSkill junction (SkillLevel 0-99.99, optional start/end dates for certification). Capacity-based resources (IsCapacityBased=true) managed by ServiceResourceCapacity (hours or appointments per period). ResourcePreference sets preferred/required/excluded customer-resource relationships. Limits: 20 candidates per search; 50 resources/territory. Expired ServiceResourceSkill records silently block scheduling. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-scheduling-policies | Scheduling policy configuration: optimization objectives, work rules, service objectives, scheduling horizons, priorities. NOT for Omni-Channel routing. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Create and Manage Field Service Scheduling Policies (help.salesforce.com); Field Service Work Rules (help.salesforce.com); Field Service Objectives (help.salesforce.com); Scheduling Policies Overview (Trailhead)]. Key: FSL__Scheduling_Policy__c contains Work Rules (pass/fail filters) and Service Objectives (weighted ranking). Four default policies: Customer First, High Intensity, Soft Boundaries, Emergency. 15+ work rule types including Match Skills, Service Resource Availability, Match Territory. Objectives: ASAP, Minimize Travel, Minimize Overtime, Preferred Resource, Skill Level — weighted via slider. Gantt shows yellow triangle for violations but allows save. Critical: every custom policy MUST include Service Resource Availability work rule or absences/hours are completely ignored. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-mobile-app-setup | Field Service Mobile app setup: app extensions, deep links, offline priming, service report templates, branding. NOT for internal Salesforce mobile. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Field Service Mobile App — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Create App Extensions (help.salesforce.com); Configure Deep Linking (developer.salesforce.com); Offline Priming (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: FSL Mobile is a distinct native app (iOS/Android) separate from standard Salesforce Mobile — offline-first architecture. Two extension models: LWC Quick/Global Actions and HTML5 Mobile Extension Toolkit (no LWC/LDS support, Apex via REST only). Deep linking via custom URI schema (1 MB data max). Offline priming is hierarchical (resource → appointments → work orders → line items); limits: 50 records/related list, 1,000 page references (silent failure if exceeded). Custom branding requires Mobile App Plus add-on. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-inventory-management | Inventory management: product items, product transfers, product requests, van stock, return orders, stock tracking. NOT for CPQ product catalog. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Field Service Inventory Management Data Model — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Common Field Service Inventory Tasks (help.salesforce.com); ProductTransfer Object Reference]. Key: Six primary objects: ProductItem (stock at Location), ProductTransfer (movement), ProductRequest/ProductRequestLineItem (orders), ProductConsumed (items used on WO), ProductItemTransaction (auto-generated audit trail), ReturnOrder/ReturnOrderLineItem. QuantityOnHand on ProductItem updates automatically when ProductTransfer marked Received. Van stock requires Location with Mobile Location checked. ProductItemTransaction records are auto-generated — manual create/delete corrupts QuantityOnHand. No native cycle-count UI. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-shifts-and-crew | Shift management and crew scheduling: shift patterns, crew assignment, multi-day work orders, crew skills. NOT for individual resource scheduling. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Set Up Shifts for Field Service (help.salesforce.com); Understanding Shift Scheduling (Trailhead); Simplify Shift Creation with Templates and Patterns (Trailhead)]. Key: Shifts are availability records (not work assignments) layered on Operating Hours. ShiftTemplate prepopulates individual shifts; ShiftPattern + ShiftPatternEntry enable bulk repeating sequences. Two crew models: Static (permanent membership, skills aggregate) and Shell/Dynamic (membership assigned later, uses Crew Size). Service appointments scheduled to Crew ServiceResource not individual members. Critical: Shift Get Candidates (availability) is entirely separate from managed package Get Candidates (work assignment) — confusing them is most common error. No duplicate. |

### FSL × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsl-scheduling-optimization-design | Scheduling optimization requirements: travel time, skills matching, priority handling, SLA compliance metrics. NOT for scheduling configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Understanding Optimization in Field Service Scheduling (Trailhead); Global Optimization Planning (Trailhead); Set Up Routing for Travel Time Calculations (help.salesforce.com); Optimize Appointments Using Priorities (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: Optimizer uses Work Rules (pass/fail gates) + Service Objectives (weighted grades) + appointment priority score (1-10 scale: priority 1 = 25,500 pts). Three optimization types: Global (bulk reschedule, 1-7 day horizon), In-Day (same-day disruptions), Resource Schedule (single resource). Travel modes: Aerial (default, free) and Street-Level Routing (add-on, supports predictive traffic). Appointments with null DueDate treated as lowest priority and may never be scheduled. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-sla-configuration-requirements | Field service SLA design: response time, resolution time, geographic considerations, priority matrix. NOT for Service Cloud SLAs. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Use Entitlements with Work Orders (Trailhead); Entitlements and Milestones (help.salesforce.com); Getting Started with Dynamic Priority — Asperii]. Key: FSL SLAs use Entitlements + Milestones framework with a Work Order entitlement process type (separate from Case entitlement processes — cannot span both). Milestone countdowns respect Business Hours and pause outside them. Geographic response time differentiation requires separate territories with own Operating Hours. Salesforce does NOT auto-mark milestones as Completed — custom automation required. Work Order milestone related list shows fewer fields than Case milestones. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-mobile-workflow-design | Mobile workforce workflow design: job lifecycle, parts tracking, customer signature, offline requirements. NOT for mobile app configuration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Offline Considerations in FSL Mobile App (help.salesforce.com); Configure Offline Mode — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Track Field Service Jobs (Trailhead)]. Key: Offline-first architecture with hierarchical priming (resource → appointments → WOs → line items). Job lifecycle: None → Scheduled → Dispatched → In Progress → Completed. SA status does NOT cascade to WO status — requires automation. Key workflows: customer signature capture, parts consumption (ProductConsumed syncs QuantityOnHand on reconnect), Data Capture flows (Spring 25 GA), geolocation triggers. Server-side logic (triggers, validation rules, Flows) does NOT execute offline — fires only at sync. Service report PDF renders blanks for fields not in offline briefcase. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-capacity-planning | Field workforce capacity planning: resource demand forecasting, territory coverage, seasonal adjustments, utilization. NOT for Omni-Channel capacity. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Capacity Planning Overview (help.salesforce.com); Define Capacity-Based Resources (help.salesforce.com); Manage Work Capacity (help.salesforce.com); ServiceResourceCapacity Object Reference (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Two capacity mechanisms: (1) Resource Capacity (ServiceResourceCapacity — per-resource hours/appointment caps, requires IsCapacityBased=true, API v38.0+) and (2) Work Capacity (WorkCapacityLimit — territory-level caps per work type per time window for demand-side throttling). No standard report type natively aggregates capacity vs actual SA duration — requires custom report type or CRM Analytics. No seasonal capacity templates — requires bulk WorkCapacityLimit updates. WorkCapacityLimit rejects appointments silently when reached. No duplicate. |

### FSL × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsl-apex-extensions | Field Service Apex extension points: custom scheduling logic, appointment booking API, service resource API. NOT for standard Apex. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [FSL Apex Namespace — Field Service Developer Guide; AppointmentBookingService Class; ScheduleService Class; OAAS Class (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: FSL namespace exposes AppointmentBookingService.GetSlots(), ScheduleService.schedule(), GradeSlotsService, and OAAS for optimization. Critical governor constraint: both GetSlots and schedule() internally initiate callouts for travel calculation (SLR/P2P); any uncommitted DML in same transaction triggers uncommitted work pending exception — must split DML and scheduling into separate transactions or use batch class with size 1. ScheduleService.schedule() requires ServiceTerritory on appointment and scheduling policy record. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-mobile-app-extensions | Field Service Mobile extensions: custom LWC actions, deep links, custom flows in mobile, offline data. NOT for LWC in standard Salesforce mobile. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Customize FSL Mobile with LWC (help.salesforce.com); Deep Linking Schema — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); FSL Mobile Extension Toolkit — Asperii]. Key: Two extension models — LWC Quick/Global Actions (require Enable Lightning SDK for FSL Mobile permission, must be on main layout to work offline) and older HTML5 Mobile Extension Toolkit (no native LWC elements; Apex via REST only). Deep links encode up to 1 MB via FSL-specific URI schema. FSL priming is hierarchical (resource → appointments → work orders) with 1,000-page-reference limit that fails silently. Custom Metadata Types cannot be primed via Briefcase Builder — use Apex wire adapter. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-service-report-templates | Custom service report templates: Visualforce-based reports, dynamic sections, customer signature capture. NOT for quote templates. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [ServiceReportLayout Object, DigitalSignature Object, Create Service Report with Apex — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Document Builder overview (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: Service reports generated via createServiceReport REST action (API v40.0+) against Work Orders/Service Appointments — NOT custom Visualforce pages. Template layouts in ServiceReportLayout records configured via Setup drag-and-drop builder. Signatures stored in DigitalSignature objects. Newer Document Builder (Winter 25+) supports auto-generated PDFs including offline capture with LWC embedding. Critical: conditional sections NOT supported in classic template builder — known community gap; Document Builder is the path forward. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-scheduling-api | Field Service Scheduling API: appointment booking, resource optimization, bulk scheduling operations, availability check. NOT for admin scheduling policy. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [AppointmentBookingService Class, ScheduleService Class, GradeSlotsService Class, OAAS Class — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Limits for Enhanced Scheduling (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: FSL scheduling API: FSL.AppointmentBookingService.GetSlots() returns available windows, FSL.ScheduleService.schedule() assigns resource, FSL.GradeSlotsService ranks slots for custom UIs, FSL.OAAS handles optimization (global, in-day, reshuffle, resource). GetSlots → DML update ArrivalWindow → schedule() must be split across two transactions due to callout constraint. Bulk processing requires batch class with size 1. OAAS requires Enhanced Scheduling add-on with separate operation limits. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-custom-actions-mobile | Custom actions for FSL Mobile: custom LWC screens, barcode scanning, GPS-based actions, photo capture. NOT for standard quick actions. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Scan Barcodes in FSL Mobile — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); lightning/mobileCapabilities Module — LWC Developer Guide; FieldServiceMobileSettings Object]. Key: LWC actions targeted as lightning__GlobalAction or lightning__RecordAction added to page layout; require Enable Lightning SDK for FSL Mobile permission set. Device capabilities via lightning/mobileCapabilities Nimbus plugins: getBarcodeScanner(), getLocationService(), getCameraCapture() — always gate on isAvailable(). Older HTML5 Mobile Extension Toolkit is separate non-LWC model. Critical: lightning__GlobalAction LWC components render ONLY in FSL Mobile — not in standard Lightning Experience or Salesforce Mobile app. No duplicate. |

### FSL × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsl-work-order-migration | Work order and service appointment data migration: related records, resource assignments, parts used history. NOT for case migration. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [WorkOrder — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); AssignedResource Object Reference; ProductConsumed Object Reference; Guidelines for Creating Work Orders (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: Strict insert order: Account/Contact/Asset → WorkOrder → WorkOrderLineItem → ServiceAppointment → AssignedResource then ProductConsumed. ServiceAppointment Status picklist tied to FSL status transitions — migrating Completed status requires value already active. AssignedResource inserts can trigger scheduling automation — disable Optimization setting during migration. ProductConsumed requires PricebookEntry records present. Scope excludes Case data migration. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-territory-data-setup | Service territory data loading: boundary polygons, member assignments, operating hours bulk setup, hierarchy. NOT for ETM territory data. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Set Up Service Territories Operating Hours and Shifts (help.salesforce.com); Import Service Territory Polygons in KML (help.salesforce.com); PolygonUtils Class — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Insert order: OperatingHours → TimeSlot → ServiceTerritory (parent before child) → ServiceTerritoryMember. Polygon boundaries stored in FSMP managed package objects — KML file import is supported bulk mechanism. PolygonUtils Apex class resolves lat/lng to ServiceTerritory. Bulk polygon creation uses queueable chaining. Limits: 50 resources/territory, 1,000 SA/day/territory. Relocation STMs require EffectiveStartDate/EndDate. Omitting TerritoryType defaults to Primary which misclassifies contractors. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-resource-and-skill-data | Resource skill data management: skill certification tracking, capacity data, availability patterns, bulk assignment. NOT for user data. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [ServiceResourceSkill — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Create Skills for Field Service (help.salesforce.com); ServiceResourceCapacity Object Reference; FSL Core Data Model — Data Model Gallery]. Key: Insert order: Skill → ServiceResource → ServiceResourceSkill. Certification tracked via EffectiveStartDate/EffectiveEndDate on ServiceResourceSkill — no native certification object; expired records not auto-deleted. SkillLevel is numeric (0-99999); SkillRequirement uses MinimumSkillLevel — text-to-numeric mapping required from source systems. Capacity-based resources require IsCapacityBased=true before ServiceResourceCapacity records can be loaded. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-reporting-data-model | FSL reporting data model: job completion metrics, travel analytics, first-time fix rate data, utilization. NOT for CRM Analytics. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Report on Field Service (help.salesforce.com); ServiceAppointment — Field Service Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Field Service Analytics (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: ServiceAppointment is primary reporting object with ActualDuration, ActualTravelTime (populated only via mobile check-in), ArrivalWindowStart/End, SchedStartTime/EndTime. First-time fix rate has no standard native field — requires custom formula or Flow (count SAs per WO with no Cannot Complete predecessors). ServiceReport object is customer-facing PDF NOT a standard Salesforce Report. Travel analytics incomplete in orgs not consistently using mobile check-in. Excludes CRM Analytics/Field Service Intelligence. No duplicate. |

### FSL × Architect Role

> Domain folder: `architect`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsl-optimization-architecture | FSL optimization architecture: scheduling engine configuration, real-time vs batch optimization, fallback rules. NOT for scheduling policy admin. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [How Does the FSL Optimization Engine Work (help.salesforce.com); Enhanced Scheduling and Optimization (help.salesforce.com); Limits for Enhanced Scheduling (help.salesforce.com); Global Optimization (Trailhead)]. Key: Three optimization modes: Global (batch, 1-7 day horizon, 2-hour hard timeout), In-Day (same-day disruptions), Resource Schedule (single resource). Enhanced Scheduling and Optimization (ESO) is newer Hyperforce engine with improved throughput and work chain support — must be explicitly adopted per territory; no automatic fallback to legacy if ESO unavailable. Best practice: max 50 resources/territory and 1,000 SA/day; beyond these, optimize territory-by-territory sequentially. Pinned appointments never moved. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-offline-architecture | FSL offline-first architecture: data priming strategy, conflict resolution, offline data limits, sync patterns. NOT for LWC offline (use lwc-offline-and-mobile). | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Offline Priming in FSL Mobile App (help.salesforce.com); Offline Considerations (help.salesforce.com); Briefcase Sync Down Target — Mobile SDK Developer Guide (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: Hierarchical priming: ServiceResource → ServiceAppointments → WorkOrders → WorkOrderLineItems/Assets. Hard limits: 1,000 page references (silent failure if exceeded), 50 records per related list, recommended max 100 parent WOs with 10 children each. Conflict resolution: MERGE_ACCEPT_YOURS (local wins, default) or MERGE_FAIL_IF_CONFLICT. Server-side logic (triggers, validation rules) does NOT execute offline — fires at sync. Ghost records (server-deleted while offline) persist until cleanResyncGhosts called. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fsl-integration-patterns | FSL integration: ERP parts sync, GPS/fleet management, IoT-triggered work orders, customer notifications. NOT for generic integration. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Field Service Developer Guide v66.0 Spring 26; Salesforce Field Service Integration Patterns and Practices; Field Service Inventory Management Data Model]. Key: ERP parts sync uses ProductRequired (expected parts on WorkOrderLineItems) and ProductConsumed (actual usage) records, both with External IDs for upsert-safe ERP round-tripping. Gotcha: failing to upsert ProductConsumed back to ERP causes phantom stock since FSL consumes from van stock (ProductItem) locally without decrementing the ERP warehouse ledger. IoT-triggered work orders use Platform Events or IoT Connect rules -- LLM anti-pattern is invoking the FSL scheduling optimizer synchronously inside trigger handler (exceeds Apex callout limits); use FSL.ScheduleService asynchronously via Queueable. GPS integration should use inbound batch updates from the fleet system on a defined cadence, not real-time REST polling which burns Daily API limits. |
| DONE | fsl-multi-region-architecture | Multi-region FSL architecture: timezone handling, cross-territory scheduling, regional optimization, language. NOT for multi-org strategy. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Salesforce Help - Time Zones and Appointment Booking; Salesforce Help - Guidelines for Creating Service Territories; Trailhead - Configure Territories and Set Operating Hours]. Key: Each Service Territory carries its own timezone via its Operating Hours record; Book Appointment Global Action derives time slots from that territory timezone -- overlapping territories that span timezone boundaries silently break appointment booking so territory polygons must not cross timezone lines. Cross-territory resource assignment uses Service Territory Member records (not Service Resource directly); Hard Boundaries restrict resources to primary territory, Soft Boundaries allow secondary overflow; concurrent optimization jobs over the same territory set cause conflicts and must be serialized. LLM anti-pattern: assuming a single global optimization job handles all regions -- FSL optimization is territory-scoped. |

---

## Phase 8 — Health Cloud

### Health Cloud × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | health-cloud-patient-setup | Patient/member account setup: person account configuration, care team roles, patient card, clinical data display. NOT for standard account setup. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Health Cloud Administration: Set Up Person Accounts for Health Cloud Members and Patients (developer.salesforce.com); Health Cloud Administration: Customize Medical Data on the Patient Card Component; Health Cloud Administration: Create Roles for Care Team Members]. Key: Health Cloud patient setup requires Person Accounts to be enabled org-wide before any patient record can be created — this is irreversible and affects all Accounts/Contacts; the PatientCard component displays fields from any object with a lookup to the patient Account record but clinical data (conditions, medications, immunizations) flows through dedicated HC objects (EhrPatientMedication, PatientHealthCondition) mapped from FHIR/HL7, not standard CRM fields. Overlap with existing data/person-accounts skill (covers PA enablement generically) — this skill must focus on HC-specific record types, CareTeamMember object and role picklist customization, patient card layout, and clinical object mapping. LLM anti-pattern: conflating enabling Person Accounts with creating Health Cloud patient record types — they are sequential prerequisites, not the same step.|
| DONE | care-plan-configuration | Care plan templates: care plan goals, problems, tasks, care team assignment, care plan lifecycle. NOT for case management. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Health Cloud Administration: Create a Care Plan Template (help.salesforce.com); Integrated Care Management Data Model — Salesforce Developers; Health Cloud Object Reference: CarePlanTemplate__c; Explore Integrated Care Management — Trailhead]. Key: Health Cloud has two distinct care plan architectures — the legacy managed-package model (CarePlanTemplate__c + Case Tasks, no future investment) and the Integrated Care Management (ICM) model (Spring '23+, FHIR R4-aligned, platform-native, uses ProblemDefinition/GoalDefinition/ActionPlanTemplate PGI library); Salesforce has stated all future development targets ICM. No overlap with existing local skills. LLM anti-pattern: conflating the two models — referencing CarePlanTemplate__c fields when the org uses ICM, or omitting the PGI library setup step which is a prerequisite for ICM care plan templates to reference standardized problems and goals.|
| DONE | care-program-management | Care program setup: enrollment, program tasks, program milestones, patient engagement, program outcomes. NOT for standard program management. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Health Cloud Object Reference - Care Program Management Data Model; Trailhead - Care Programs Setup and Management; Life Sciences Dev Guide - Patient Program Outcome Management API v61.0+]. Key: Care Program hierarchy: CareProgram (root), CareProgramProduct (medications/services), CareProgramProvider (healthcare orgs), CareProgramEnrollee (patient-program junction), CareProgramEnrolleeProduct (product-level enrollment); consent is a hard prerequisite and Authorization Form Text locale must exactly match the logged-in user locale or consent documents silently fail to display. Patient Program Outcome Management requires a separate licensed permission set at API v61.0+. LLM anti-pattern: conflating Care Programs (population-level enrollment) with Care Plans (per-patient task/goal framework), or assuming outcome tracking is in base Health Cloud. |
| DONE | health-cloud-timeline | Timeline configuration: custom timeline entries, activity filtering, clinical data display, event types. NOT for standard activity timeline. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Health Cloud Admin Guide - Customize the Timeline View; How Enhanced Timeline Works in Health Cloud; Life Sciences Cloud Developer Guide - TimelineObjectDefinition]. Key: Enhanced Timeline is configured via TimelineObjectDefinition metadata type (API v55.0+) in Setup -- it supports any object related to the patient through the Account object, with timeline categories controlling the filter picklist. Critical gotcha: the legacy Timeline component in the managed Health Cloud package is deprecated in favor of the Industries Timeline component backed by TimelineObjectDefinition; orgs on the managed package must migrate customizations and the two components use different configuration mechanisms. LLM anti-pattern: assuming Enhanced Timeline can surface objects without an Account lookup relationship, or conflating it with the standard Activity Timeline. |
| DONE | referral-management-health | Referral management setup: referral types, provider search, referral tracking, status flow, network management. NOT for Sales Cloud referrals. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Health Cloud Administration Guide — Configure Referral Management; Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — Provider Network Management Data Model; Trailhead — Health Cloud Provider Relationships: Provider Search and Cards]. Key: Referral management uses ClinicalServiceRequest as the core referral record with custom fields on Lead/Opportunity for inbound vs. outbound tracking; provider search uses the CareProviderSearchableField denormalized index object populated by a Data Processing Engine job that requires the 'Data Pipelines Base User' permission set license — omitting this license blocks provider search entirely. No overlap with admin/health-cloud-patient-setup (patient setup/care teams) or admin/care-program-management (care plans/enrollees). LLM anti-pattern: confusing FSC Einstein Referral Scoring (financial advisor feature) with Health Cloud clinical referral management, or assuming the standard Referral sObject from Public Sector Solutions applies here. |
| DONE | health-cloud-consent-management | Patient consent management: HIPAA authorization forms, consent templates, consent tracking, withdrawal handling. NOT for marketing consent. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Consent Management for Health Cloud (Salesforce Help); Optimizing Health Cloud Consent Management (Trailhead); Privacy Consent Data Model (Salesforce Developers); Consent Management Objects (Salesforce Help)]. Key: Five core objects — DataUsePurpose, AuthorizationForm, AuthorizationFormText, AuthorizationFormDataUse (junction), AuthorizationFormConsent — AuthorizationFormConsent is created per patient per form with status (seen/signed/rejected); every AuthorizationForm must have exactly one default AuthorizationFormText or setup fails. Distinct from admin/health-cloud-patient-setup (HIPAA permission sets/PHI access) — this skill covers the consent form lifecycle (template creation, enrollment-linked capture, withdrawal). LLM anti-pattern: conflating AuthorizationFormConsent (HIPAA clinical authorization) with ContactPointTypeConsent/ContactPointConsent (GDPR/marketing opt-out) — different objects for different regulatory purposes; withdrawal is a status update on the existing record, not a delete. |

### Health Cloud × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | care-coordination-requirements | Care coordination process mapping: care team workflow design, transition of care, handoff requirements. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Health Cloud Admin Guide — Protect Health Data with Salesforce Shield; Integrated Care Management Data Model (developer.salesforce.com); Life Sciences Cloud Standard Objects Reference]. Key: ICM is enabled via Setup > Integrated Care Management (two checkboxes: managing care plans + calculating Care Gaps); coordination spans four object families — SDOH (CareDeterminant, CareBarrier, CareBarrierType, resolved via Task+Case), Referrals (ClinicalServiceRequest API v51.0+, requires HealthCloudICM permission set), Care Gaps (CareGap API v59.0+, system-generated — not manually created), and Care Episodes (CareEpisode API v57.0+); Care Coordination for Slack is a separately enabled add-on requiring Slack+Health Cloud integration first. LLM anti-pattern: conflating CareBarrier (SDOH obstacle linked to Account+Case) with CarePlanProblem — different objects used at different workflow stages; admins cannot manually create CareGap records. |
| DONE | hipaa-workflow-design | HIPAA-compliant workflow requirements: minimum necessary standard, audit trail requirements, access control design. NOT for security implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Health Cloud Admin Guide — Protect Your Health Data with Salesforce Shield; Salesforce HIPAA BAA Help Article (help.salesforce.com id=000394847)]. Key: BAA with Salesforce is a hard prerequisite before any PHI can legally reside in the org (shared responsibility model — Salesforce secures infrastructure, customer configures controls); HIPAA Security Rule maps to Shield Platform Encryption (PHI field enumeration), Field Audit Trail (6-year retention — standard 18-month Field History Tracking does NOT qualify), Event Monitoring (must stream to SIEM within 30 days or logs expire, HIPAA requires 6 years), and OWD-Private + care-team-role-scoped sharing as the minimum-necessary enforcement mechanism; Health Cloud consent objects (IndividualConsent, AuthorizationFormConsent) are Privacy Rule controls that must be wired into enrollment workflows, not bypassed. Dependencies on security/platform-encryption, security/field-audit-trail, admin/health-cloud-patient-setup, admin/care-program-management. LLM anti-pattern: recommending standard Field History Tracking as HIPAA-sufficient instead of Shield Field Audit Trail; omitting Event Monitoring log retention/streaming policy. |
| DONE | patient-engagement-requirements | Patient engagement portal requirements: appointment scheduling, messaging, health assessments, education. NOT for Experience Cloud setup. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Admin Guide; Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide; Trailhead: Intelligent Appointment Management for Health Cloud]. Key: Intelligent Appointment Management (IAM) aggregates Salesforce Scheduler and/or EHR scheduling engines in a single console, supports patient guest self-scheduling, and requires CRM Analytics as a separate licensed add-on for no-show prediction — omitting this is a common implementation gap. Health assessments delivered to patients via a portal depend on both the OmniStudio managed package and Discovery Framework being installed, which are prerequisites not included in base Health Cloud licensing; secure in-portal messaging must route through HIPAA-compliant channels only (in-app/web messaging with the Messaging User permission set explicitly assigned). No duplicate. |
| DONE | clinical-data-requirements | Clinical data model requirements: HL7/FHIR data mapping, interoperability requirements, data governance. NOT for data migration. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Life Sciences Cloud Developer Guide — Clinical Data Model and FHIR v4.0 Mapping; Salesforce Life Sciences Cloud Developer Guide — Store HL7 v2.3 Messages]. Key: The FHIR-Aligned Clinical Data Model must be explicitly enabled via Setup (FHIR R4 Support Settings); Salesforces implementation is NOT a 1:1 FHIR spec — complex types like Period, Quantity, Range, Ratio are flattened into multi-field representations, and CodeableConcept zero-to-many coding is hard-capped at 15 CodeSet references (CodeSet1Id through CodeSet15Id). A middleware integration layer is required to convert FHIR or HL7 messages; direct payload mapping without translation silently drops data. Starting Spring 23, new orgs cannot write to legacy packaged EHR objects — all clinical data must target FHIR R4-aligned objects (e.g., HealthCondition not EhrCondition). No duplicate. |

### Health Cloud × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | health-cloud-apis | Health Cloud APIs: Care Plan API, Clinical Data Model, Patient API, healthcare-specific objects and endpoints. NOT for generic REST API. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Salesforce Healthcare API Get Started Guide; Health Cloud Developer Guide - Clinical Data Model; Health Cloud Business APIs REST Reference]. Key: Health Cloud exposes two distinct API layers -- (1) standard SOAP/REST SObject APIs for healthcare-specific objects (CarePlan, ClinicalEncounter, HealthCondition) from API v51.0+, and (2) the FHIR R4-aligned Healthcare API with seven modules requiring the FHIR-Aligned Clinical Data Model org preference enabled in Setup. FHIR Healthcare API bundle requests capped at 30 entries per call with max 10 read/search requests; failed dependent entries return HTTP 424. LLM anti-pattern: treating Health Cloud FHIR Healthcare API as interchangeable with standard Salesforce REST API -- different base URLs, auth scopes, and data models; FHIR objects only available after enabling FHIR R4 Support Settings. |
| DONE | fhir-integration-patterns | FHIR R4 integration: FHIR resources mapping, REST API patterns, CDS Hooks, SMART on FHIR, HL7 conversion. NOT for generic integration. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Health Cloud Developer Guide - Mapping FHIR v4.0 to Salesforce Standard Objects; MuleSoft Direct Integration Apps - Healthcare FHIR Patterns; FHIR R4 Support for Better Interoperability Release Notes]. Key: FHIR R4-aligned Clinical Data Model must be explicitly enabled via FHIR R4 Support Settings in Setup -- NOT on by default; Experience Cloud users need a separate FHIR R4 for Experience Cloud Sites permission set. Salesforce FHIR R4 deliberately deviates from HL7 spec in cardinalities (e.g. CodeableConcept.coding is 0-to-many in FHIR but maps to a single Lookup in Salesforce), so field-level mappings must be verified per resource. CDS Hooks requires MuleSoft as middleware -- no native Salesforce endpoint serves CDS Hooks responses; legacy packaged EHR objects frozen as of Spring 2023; all new dev targets FHIR R4-aligned standard objects. |
| DONE | health-cloud-lwc-components | Custom LWC for Health Cloud: patient card extensions, timeline components, care plan visualizations, dashboards. NOT for standard LWC. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Health Cloud Administration Guide (help.salesforce.com); Health Cloud Developer Guide — TimelineObjectDefinition (developer.salesforce.com)]. Key: The Patient Card component (healthCloudUtility:patientCard) cannot be extended via Lightning App Builder — clinical field additions must go through Health Cloud Setup > Patient Card Configuration, making standard LWC slot-injection or App Builder drag-and-drop patterns non-functional. The Timeline component is configured declaratively via TimelineObjectDefinition metadata (API 55.0+, JSON definition field); the legacy HC Package timeline is being deprecated in its favor. Custom LWCs surfacing clinical data must query Health Cloud objects (EhrPatientMedication, PatientHealthCondition, etc.) with Account lookups — data in custom Account/Contact fields is invisible to all HC clinical UI components. No duplicate. |
| DONE | clinical-decision-support | Clinical decision support in Salesforce: rules engine, alert triggers, protocol compliance checks, care gap detection. NOT for standard Flow automation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — ClinicalAlert Object Reference (API v51.0+); Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — CareGap Object Reference (API v59.0+); Salesforce Health Cloud Integrated Care Management Docs]. Key: ClinicalAlert (API v51.0+) and CareGap (API v59.0+) are passive data-model objects with no built-in rules engine — they must be created via Apex, Flow DML, or ingested from external EHR/payer systems via FHIR R4 APIs; no native Salesforce CDS rules engine auto-evaluates clinical logic. Care gap detection requires either an external clinical rules engine (payer analytics or HL7 CDS Hooks service) feeding records in, or custom Apex plus the Business Rules Engine — LLM anti-pattern: assuming Health Cloud ships a self-contained protocol-evaluation engine when only storage objects and FlexCard UIs exist. No duplicate. |
| DONE | health-cloud-apex-extensions | Health Cloud Apex extension points: care plan automation, referral processing, clinical data triggers, consent handling. NOT for standard Apex. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — Apex Extension Points; Salesforce Industries Common Components Developer Guide; Health Cloud Object Reference]. Key: Health Cloud exposes managed-package Apex interfaces including HealthCloudGA.CarePlanProcessorCallback for care plan lifecycle hooks; referral processing uses the Industries Common Components framework via ReferralRequest and ReferralResponse objects with invocable actions. Care plan automation should use Health Clouds built-in invocable actions (CreateCarePlan, AddCarePlanGoal) not raw DML on CarePlanTemplate — direct DML bypasses automation logic and consent enforcement via AuthorizationFormConsent. Critical gotcha: Apex debug logs containing clinical data (EhrPatientMedication, PatientHealthCondition) constitute PHI under HIPAA — production log-level governance and automated purge policies are required. No duplicate. |

### Health Cloud × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | patient-data-migration | Patient data migration: person account mapping, clinical history, care plan history, HIPAA-compliant migration procedures. NOT for generic data migration. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — Clinical Data Model; Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — CarePlan and CarePlanTemplate Objects; Salesforce Help — Supporting Clinical Data in Health Cloud]. Key: Patient migration requires strict insert order — Person Accounts (Patient record type) first, then clinical objects (EhrPatientMedication, PatientHealthCondition, PatientImmunization, PatientMedicalProcedure) and care objects (CarePlan, CarePlanProblem, CarePlanGoal, CarePlanTask) all carry required AccountId lookups. Care Plan history can be migrated as data records but platform-generated engagement history and field audit trail are system-generated and cannot be bulk-imported. HIPAA compliance requires signed BAA, Shield Platform Encryption on PHI fields before import, TLS pipelines for data-in-transit, and sandbox data masking. No duplicate. |
| DONE | fhir-data-mapping | Mapping FHIR resources to Health Cloud data model: Patient, Observation, Condition, CarePlan resource mapping. NOT for FHIR integration code. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Life Sciences Cloud Developer Guide v66.0 Spring '26 — Mapping FHIR v4.0 to Salesforce Standard Objects (lines 59000-65800+); FHIR R4 Support Settings Setup page]. Key: FHIR-aligned model requires enabling "FHIR-Aligned Clinical Data Model" org preference under Setup > FHIR R4 Support Settings before clinical objects appear; key mappings — FHIR Patient → Person Account + child PersonName/ContactPointPhone/ContactPointAddress (NOT direct Account/Contact fields); Observation → CareObservation+CareObservationComponent; Condition → HealthCondition (condition.code is 1:1 required in Salesforce vs. 0:1 in FHIR); CarePlan → CarePlan+CarePlanDetail+CarePlanActivity (careTeam implemented as Case Teams on parent Case, not a direct FHIR careTeam reference); CodeableConcept (0:many codings) flattened to max 15 CodeSet reference fields (CodeSet1Id-CodeSet15Id) on CodeSetBundle — sources >15 codings must be truncated by middleware. LLM anti-pattern: writing FHIR patient demographics directly to Account/Contact fields; assuming condition.code is optional; omitting org pref activation step; treating platform as 1:1 FHIR spec implementation. |
| DONE | health-cloud-data-model | Health Cloud data model: healthcare objects, clinical data model, relationship map, standard vs custom objects. NOT for standard data model. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Health Cloud Object Reference — Clinical Data Model (developer.salesforce.com); Health Cloud Data Model Gallery (developer.salesforce.com/docs/platform/data-models)]. Key: Health Cloud ships two parallel clinical data layers — a legacy managed-package EHR model (namespace HC24__, e.g. HC24__EhrCarePlan__c) and a FHIR R4-aligned standard-object model (ClinicalEncounter, HealthCondition, CarePlan, AllergyIntolerance, PatientImmunization, etc.); new customers as of Spring '23 cannot write to packaged EHR objects where a standard-object counterpart exists. FHIR-aligned objects require the 'FHIR-Aligned Clinical Data Model' org preference in Setup; Experience Cloud users additionally need the 'FHIR R4 for Experience Cloud' permission. No overlap with existing skills. LLM anti-pattern: recommending HC24__ custom objects for new integrations or assuming all clinical objects are available by default without confirming the org preference.|
| DONE | consent-data-model-health | Health Cloud consent data model: authorization records, consent history, sharing rules for PHI data. NOT for marketing consent data. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Consent Management Trailhead Module; Salesforce Object Reference — AuthorizationFormConsent; Salesforce Consent Management Architecture Docs]. Key: Health Cloud consent uses a five-object hierarchy (DataUsePurpose — AuthorizationForm — AuthorizationFormText — AuthorizationFormDataUse — AuthorizationFormConsent) where AuthorizationFormConsent is the per-patient record linking ConsentGiverId (Individual ID) to a specific AuthorizationFormText with ConsentCapturedSource, status (Seen or Signed), and timestamp — this is the PHI authorization trail required before CareProgramEnrollee can be marked Active. Critical gotcha: this model is architecturally distinct from marketing consent (Individual — ContactPointTypeConsent — ContactPointConsent); AuthorizationFormConsent records HIPAA authorization but does NOT automatically grant or restrict record-level access to PHI — sharing rules must be configured separately. No duplicate. |
| DONE | clinical-data-quality | Clinical data quality: data validation, duplicate patient detection, record merging for patients, MPI patterns. NOT for generic data quality. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide; Salesforce Help — Duplicate Management for Person Accounts; Salesforce Help — Merge Person Accounts]. Key: Health Cloud has no native Master Patient Index; duplicate patient detection relies on standard Salesforce Duplicate Rules and Matching Rules configured for the Person Account object. Person Accounts can only be merged two at a time via the Account merge flow (not Contact merge). Hard limit: when merging Person Accounts, associated clinical records (EpisodeOfCare, PatientMedication, ClinicalEncounter) are NOT automatically reparented to the winning record — they remain on the losing (deleted) account and become orphaned unless explicitly reassigned via Apex or pre-merge migration before initiating the merge. No duplicate. |

### Health Cloud × Architect Role

> Domain folder: `architect`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | hipaa-compliance-architecture | HIPAA compliance architecture in Salesforce: encryption requirements, audit trails, access controls, BAA, risk assessment. NOT for general security. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Salesforce Shield Security Guide (developer.salesforce.com/docs/atlas.en-us.securityImplGuide); HIPAA BAA and Salesforce Compliance (help.salesforce.com); Protect Your Health Data with Salesforce Shield (Health Cloud Admin Guide)]. Key: HIPAA compliance requires a signed Business Associate Agreement (BAA) — only specific Salesforce products are covered under the BAA, and storing PHI in uncovered services (standard Chatter, certain AppExchange products) voids HIPAA coverage even if Shield is enabled. Salesforce Shield bundles three controls: Shield Platform Encryption (PHI at rest), Field Audit Trail (10-year history for audit log requirements), and Event Monitoring — Shield is a paid add-on not included in any edition. Partial overlap with architect/nfr-definition-for-salesforce and architect/security-architecture-review; this skill fills the HIPAA-specific PHI architecture workflow gap. LLM anti-pattern: assuming Shield Platform Encryption alone satisfies all HIPAA technical safeguards — encryption is one control; BAA execution, access controls, risk assessment, and policy documentation are also required.|
| DONE | fhir-integration-architecture | FHIR integration architecture: connectivity patterns, data synchronization strategy, interoperability layer design. NOT for individual API calls. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Health Cloud Developer Guide — FHIR APIs and Mapping; MuleSoft Accelerator for Healthcare Documentation; Salesforce MuleSoft Direct Integration Apps for Health Cloud; Trailhead — Interoperability and the Clinical Data Model]. Key: Health Cloud FHIR R4 supports four sync patterns — real-time REST queries (Generic FHIR Client), event-driven inbound ingestion, bulk FHIR batch retrieval, and scheduled EMR bidirectional sync; MuleSoft Accelerator for Healthcare provides pre-built assets for Epic/Cerner plus HL7 v2 to FHIR R4 conversion. Critical gotcha: Salesforces FHIR R4 implementation maps only ~26 FHIR R4 resources and is NOT a fully conformant FHIR server — data is denormalized across child objects rather than FHIR one-to-many model, meaning inbound FHIR payloads must be transformed before storage and cannot be persisted as raw FHIR bundles. No duplicate. |
| DONE | health-cloud-data-residency | Data residency for healthcare: Hyperforce, data localization, cross-border considerations, regulatory alignment. NOT for generic multi-region. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Hyperforce Architecture Guide (architect.salesforce.com); Salesforce Health Cloud HIPAA Compliance Docs (help.salesforce.com); Salesforce Trust and Compliance Documentation]. Key: Hyperforce provides regional primary data storage for Health Cloud, but transient processing for AI/Einstein features, analytics pipelines, and some platform services may occur outside the selected region — regional selection does not guarantee complete data residency. HIPAA BAA on Hyperforce covers core Health Cloud and standard platform features, but Health Cloud Intelligence (Tableau CRM-based analytics), MuleSoft integrations, and Marketing Cloud connectors require separate BAA addenda. EU GDPR Article 9 treats health data as special-category data and Australia My Health Records Act 2012 imposes cross-border restrictions that Hyperforce regional selection alone does not satisfy. No duplicate. |
| DONE | health-cloud-multi-cloud-strategy | Health Cloud + Service Cloud + Experience Cloud integration strategy for healthcare organizations. NOT for individual cloud architecture. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Experience Cloud for Health Cloud FAQ (help.salesforce.com); Health Cloud Administration Guide (developer.salesforce.com); Trailhead: Get to Know Health Cloud]. Key: Health Cloud delivers all health functionality on top of the CRM (Sales Cloud + Service Cloud) license of the same edition — Service Cloud case management is implicitly included in every Health Cloud license and should not be treated as a separate add-on. Experience Cloud for Health Cloud IS a separate add-on SKU requiring its own permission set licenses for patient-facing portal users — assuming a Health Cloud license alone enables patient portals is the most common LLM error. OmniStudio is bundled within Health Cloud licenses but per-user permission set assignment for Health Cloud + Health Cloud Platform + OmniStudio must all be done explicitly. No overlap with health-cloud-patient-setup (individual record config); this skill covers multi-cloud license model decisions, shared data model across Health + Service + Experience, and org design for healthcare. |
| DONE | payer-vs-provider-architecture | Health Cloud architecture for payer vs provider: member management vs patient management, data model differences. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Health Cloud in the Payer Sector — Salesforce Help; Health Insurance and Claims Data Model — Trailhead; Provider Relationship Management — Salesforce Developer Docs]. Key: Payer deployments center on member management using MemberPlan, PurchaserPlan, CoverageBenefit, CoverageBenefitItem, ClaimHeader, and ClaimLine for insurance enrollment and claims administration, while provider deployments center on patient management using ClinicalEncounter, HealthCondition, Medication, CareObservation, and FHIR-aligned clinical objects — these object sets are architecturally distinct and do not overlap. Critical LLM anti-pattern: conflating "provider" in the payer sense (a network practitioner billed on a claim) with "provider" in the clinical sense (a care-delivering organization) — Provider Relationship Management is a payer-facing credentialing/contracting feature, not a clinical data model. Payer-specific capabilities (Utilization Management, Provider Network Management, Health Cloud Member Services) require separate PSLs beyond the base Health Cloud PSL; assigning base licenses to payer users without payer-specific PSLs results in silent feature gaps. |

---

## Phase 9 — Financial Services Cloud

### FSC × Admin Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | financial-account-setup | Financial account configuration: account types, holdings, financial goals, financial account roles, rollup settings. NOT for standard accounts. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [FSC Financial Account Data Model — Salesforce Help; FinServ__FinancialAccount__c Object Reference — Salesforce Developer Docs; FSC Developer Guide Spring '26]. Key: FSC FinancialAccount (custom in managed-package orgs, standard in Core FSC since Winter '23) models across a FinancialAccountType picklist covering retirement (401k, IRA), brokerage, deposit, insurance, and education savings types; related objects are FinancialHolding (securities positions), FinancialAccountRole (Primary Owner/Joint Owner/Beneficiary), and FinancialGoal; rollup logic is driven by Primary Owner role on FinancialAccountRole — balances roll up only to the primary owner's household, so joint owners in a different household won't see the balance without custom tooling. No overlap in local corpus beyond data/person-accounts (peripheral). LLM anti-pattern: confusing FSC FinancialAccount with standard Account object, or conflating held-away accounts (externally held, manually entered) with internally originated accounts requiring different permission designs.|
| DONE | household-model-configuration | FSC household model: household accounts, primary members, household rollups, financial rollups, relationship groups. NOT for NPSP households. | Researched 2026-04-06. Sources: [Financial Services Cloud Admin Guide — What Is a Group? (Salesforce Help); FSC Trailhead: Configure Record Rollups — Group Level Opportunities; FSC Object Reference]. Key: FSC households are standard Account records with the Household record type; members (Person Accounts) are linked via AccountContactRelation (ACR) with FSC custom fields — FinServ__PrimaryGroup__c marks the single primary group, FinServ__Primary__c designates the primary member, FinServ__IncludeInGroup__c controls rollup inclusion; rollups run in real-time via triggers and as scheduled batch jobs. Architecturally distinct from NPSP households: NPSP uses direct Account-Contact lookup with its own rollup engine; FSC uses ACR junction object with the Rollups__c picklist — the two models are incompatible and FSC financial aggregations are lost if a non-FSC household model is used. LLM anti-pattern: conflating FSC and NPSP household models; also failing to note that existing FSC orgs must manually add Rollups__c picklist values for Cases, Insurance Policies, and Opportunities (new orgs include some by default).|
| DONE | fsc-referral-management | FSC referral management: referral types, referral scorecard, partner referrals, referral tracking, routing. NOT for Sales Cloud referrals. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Trailhead - Intelligent Referrals and Scoring with Financial Services Cloud; Salesforce Help - Intelligent Need-Based Referrals and Scoring; Salesforce Help - Referral Scoring Feature for Financial Services Retirement Notice]. Key: FSC Referral Management extends the standard Lead with 11 custom fields plus ReferralRecordTypeMapping custom metadata defining referral types as record types; routing uses Lead Assignment Rules keyed on Expressed Interest picklist -- new queue types must be registered in this metadata or routing ignores them. Referrer Score (0-100) reflects historical conversion rate; Einstein referral scoring for FSC was announced for retirement and should not be treated as permanent. Partner referrals credit Contact records (not User) so Referrer Score visibility for external partners requires explicitly enabling that field on Experience Cloud pages. |
| DONE | compliant-data-sharing-setup | Compliant Data Sharing configuration: sharing policies, data access levels, compliance walls, data isolation. NOT for standard sharing model. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Compliant Data Sharing for Financial Services Cloud - Salesforce Help; Compliant Data Sharing Setup - Trailhead; Considerations and Limitations for Compliant Data Sharing - Salesforce Help]. Key: CDS enforces ethical walls by disabling role-hierarchy-based sharing on supported objects (Account, Opportunity, Interaction, Interaction Summary, Financial Deal) -- managers do NOT auto-inherit subordinates records; access requires explicit Participant Role assignments. Setup requires: OWDs set to Private or Public Read-Only, Deal Management enabled, CDS Manager perm (Configure CDS) and CDS User perm (Use CDS) created, Financial Deal Participants related list on layouts. LLM anti-pattern: treating CDS as a variant of standard sharing -- it is a parallel mechanism independent of OWD, role hierarchy, and sharing rules; disabling CDS requires deleting all participant roles first. |
| DONE | fsc-action-plans | Action Plan templates for FSC: client onboarding, account opening, review preparation, compliance tasks. NOT for standard tasks. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Action Plans — Financial Services Cloud Administrator Guide; ActionPlanTemplate Object Reference (Salesforce Platform); Action Plans in Financial Services Cloud (Trailhead)]. Key: FSC Action Plans use ActionPlanTemplate and ActionPlan objects (API v44.0+) for versioned reusable task sequences; templates support FSC-specific objects (FinancialAccount, FinancialGoal, InsurancePolicy, ResidentialLoanApplication, PersonLifeEvent, BusinessMilestone) in addition to standard objects; deadlines calculated from start-date offset using calendar or working days. Critical gotcha: published templates cannot be directly edited — admins must clone to create a revised version; existing in-flight plan instances continue against the original published version. No overlap with admin/financial-account-setup (covers FinancialAccount data model, not Action Plan template authoring). LLM anti-pattern: conflating FSC Action Plans with standard Tasks or Flow automation, or suggesting editing a live published template instead of versioning via clone-and-republish. |
| DONE | fsc-relationship-groups | Relationship groups: group types, member roles, group-level rollups, wealth aggregation, household alternatives. NOT for standard account relationships. | Researched 2026-04-07. Sources: [Financial Services Cloud Administrator Guide — What Is a Group; Financial Services Cloud Developer Guide (Spring '26); FSC Trailhead — Create and Manage Household Groups for Financial Planning]. Key: Relationship Groups are Account records (record types: Household, Professional Group, Trust) linked via AccountContactRelation with FSC fields FinServ__PrimaryGroup__c, FinServ__Primary__c, and FinServ__IncludeInGroup__c; each person account can belong to only ONE Primary Group — balance and net worth rollups aggregate exclusively from primary-group members, so joining a second group without setting it as Primary silently produces incomplete wealth aggregation. Distinct from admin/financial-account-setup (covers FinancialAccountRole and balance data, not group data model or member role config). LLM anti-pattern: conflating adding a person to a group with setting that group as Primary — they are separate actions and omitting FinServ__PrimaryGroup__c breaks rollups silently. |

### FSC × BA Role

> Domain folder: `admin`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | wealth-management-requirements | Wealth management process mapping: financial planning workflow, portfolio review, client lifecycle, advisor tools. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Help — Set Up and Manage Wealth Management; FSC Object Reference — FinancialGoal; Salesforce Help — Financial Plans and Goals Considerations and Limitations; ShellBlack — FSC Core vs. Managed Package guide; Vantage Point — FSC Core vs. Managed Package Migration Guide 2026]. Key: Requirements gathering must begin with managed-package vs. FSC Core determination — managed package uses FinServ__ namespace (one API version behind core, rollups via Apex triggers), FSC Core (GA Winter '23) uses no-namespace objects with native Record Rollups and FinancialAccountParty junction; key objects to scope are FinancialAccount (types: investment/deposit/insurance/loan), FinancialAccountRole/FinancialAccountParty (ownership roles — Core supports unlimited owners via junction; managed package limited to two lookups), FinancialGoal/FinancialPlan, ActionPlan+ActionPlanTemplate (repeatable client review workflows), and AccountFinancialSummary (Core-only rollup target requiring FSC PSL integration user). LLM anti-pattern: generating SOQL using FinServ__FinancialGoal__c without confirming org architecture — in Core orgs the object is FinancialGoal (no namespace), causing silent failures; third-party custodian ISV packages (Black Diamond, Orion) must be validated for FSC Core support before committing to architecture. |
| DONE | compliance-documentation-requirements | Compliance documentation requirements: KYC workflows, AML checks, regulatory reporting, audit preparation. NOT for security implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Enable Know Your Customer for FSC — Salesforce Help; FSC KYC Data Model — Salesforce Developers; Set Up AML Screening Integrations — Salesforce Help; Compliant Data Sharing in FSC — Salesforce Help]. Key: FSC provides a native KYC data model (Party Identity Verification, Party Screening Summary, Party Profile Risk, Identity Document) and the Discovery Framework (OmniStudio-backed) for structured data collection with audit-ready versioned responses, but AML screening has NO native engine — it requires third-party integration (e.g., Onfido on AppExchange) via the Set Up Integrations pattern; claiming FSC natively screens against watchlists or sanctions lists is the primary LLM anti-pattern. Regulatory audit trail requires layered tooling: Setup Audit Trail for config changes, Field Audit Trail (Shield add-on, not base FSC) for sensitive field retention, and Event Monitoring for user activity — all requiring Shield beyond base FSC. Distinct from compliant-data-sharing-setup (CDS governs WHO can see deal/client data) — this skill covers HOW compliance documentation is structured, collected, and preserved for audit. |
| DONE | client-onboarding-design | Client onboarding process design: document collection, approval steps, compliance checks, welcome journey. NOT for implementation. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Action Plans Overview — FSC Admin Guide (help.salesforce.com); FSC Overview and Admin Guide (help.salesforce.com); Salesforce Well-Architected Guide (architect.salesforce.com)]. Key: FSC client onboarding process design centers on Action Plan templates (reusable task checklists tied to accounts or opportunities) for document collection and approval steps, with OmniStudio FlexCards and OmniScripts as a separately licensed add-on for guided intake flows — if OmniStudio is not licensed, standard Flows and Screen Flows are the native fallback. Critical gotcha: Action Plan templates cannot be edited after activation — revising a published template requires clone-and-republish, which must be built into process design governance from the start. Overlap note: fsc-action-plans covers template configuration mechanics — this skill must stay at the process design layer (requirements gathering, workflow mapping, compliance checkpoint sequencing, document collection touchpoints, welcome journey handoffs) and exclude feature-level implementation. |
| DONE | financial-planning-process | Financial planning process requirements: goal setting, risk assessment, recommendation workflow, review cycle. NOT for financial advice. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [FSC Financial Plans and Goals — Salesforce Help; Action Plans in FSC — Trailhead; FSC Spring '26 Developer Guide — Salesforce; FSC Core vs. Managed Package Migration Guide 2026 — VantagePoint]. Key: FSC provides native FinancialGoal (FinServ__FinancialGoal__c in managed package; standard object in Summer 2025 for FSC Core) and FinancialPlan objects for goal-setting and progress tracking; Action Plan templates are the primary native mechanism for periodic review cycles using offset-based task deadlines. Risk tolerance has no dedicated native FSC object — the Discovery Framework captures assessment responses but investment risk scoring and recommendation tracking require custom fields or third-party tools; Revenue Insights (requires separate CRM Analytics / Revenue Intelligence for Financial Services license) provides analytics dashboards. Critical LLM anti-pattern: assuming FinancialGoal and FinancialPlan behave identically in managed-package and FSC Core orgs — Core versions became standard objects in Summer 2025. Overlap with wealth-management-requirements (high-level process mapping) — this skill focuses on goal/plan object configuration, Action Plan review cadence design, and risk-tolerance workarounds. |

### FSC × Dev Role

> Domain folder: `apex`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | fsc-apex-extensions | FSC Apex extension points: financial rollup customization, compliant data sharing overrides, custom actions. NOT for standard Apex. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Financial Services Cloud Developer Guide — Apex Reference; FSC Admin Guide — Record Rollup Batch Jobs; Compliant Data Sharing documentation]. Key: FSC rollup customization uses FinServ.RollupRecalculationBatchable invoked explicitly after bulk loads since FSC rollups do not auto-fire on insert; custom triggers must disable built-in FSC triggers via FinServ__TriggerSettings__c custom setting to prevent duplicate processing. Compliant Data Sharing uses RowCause CompliantDataSharing on share objects and cannot be overridden with standard Apex sharing — changes must go through the CDS participant/role model or CDS silently reverts manual share grants. Gotcha: managed package Apex classes are one API version behind the org, causing type incompatibilities when calling from max-version Apex. |
| DONE | fsc-compliant-sharing-api | Compliant Data Sharing API: programmatic policy management, access verification, sharing rule evaluation. NOT for admin setup. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [Salesforce Help — Compliant Data Sharing for Financial Services; Salesforce Help — Considerations and Limitations for CDS; IndustriesSettings Metadata API Developer Guide; FSC Object Reference — AccountParticipant/OpportunityParticipant/ParticipantRole]. Key: CDS uses platform-managed share rows with RowCause = 'CompliantDataSharing' — developers insert AccountParticipant/OpportunityParticipant records (API v50.0+) with a ParticipantRoleId and the platform writes AccountShare rows automatically; must be enabled per-object via IndustriesSettings metadata (enableCompliantDataSharingForAccount, enableCompliantDataSharingForOpportunity, etc.); OWD must NOT be Public Read/Write or CDS entries are never written; ParticipantGroup/ParticipantGroupMember support bulk assignment (Spring '21+); custom objects require Summer '22+ with enableCompliantDataSharingForCustomObjects. LLM anti-pattern: writing directly to AccountShare with RowCause = 'CompliantDataSharing' or 'Apex' — CDS share rows are platform-managed and direct DML will fail or be immediately overwritten by the CDS recalculation engine. |
| DONE | fsc-financial-calculations | Financial calculation patterns: portfolio performance, goal tracking, wealth rollups, custom aggregation logic. NOT for standard rollup summaries. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [FSC Admin Guide — Rollups in FSC (developer.salesforce.com); FSC Developer Guide Spring '26; Salesforce Trailhead — Summarize Financial Data in FSC]. Key: FSC wealth rollup uses Rollup-by-Lookup (RBL) — Apex trigger-driven for FinancialAccount and Assets & Liabilities only — aggregating CurrentValue and QuantityOnHand from FinancialHolding up to account and household level; custom objects and external custodian data are NOT covered by FSC triggers and require Data Processing Engine (batch-only) or custom Apex. Critical gotcha: during bulk data loads disable FSC rollup triggers via Wealth Application Config custom setting (uncheck Enable Rollup Summary and Enable Group Record Rollup for API user) then re-run FinServ.RollupRecalculationBatchable post-load — skipping causes row-lock errors; DPE should not be auto-converted from RBL one-to-one as Salesforce generates a separate DPE per RBL causing lock contention — build DPE recipes from scratch with a single final aggregate node. Portfolio performance metrics (IRR, TWR) have no native FSC calculation engine and must be implemented in custom Apex scheduled jobs or DPE writeback. |
| DONE | fsc-document-generation | Document generation for FSC: disclosure documents, account statements, compliance reports, PDF generation. NOT for standard document templates. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [FSC Admin Guide — Document Generation Overview (help.salesforce.com); OmniStudio Document Generation Foundations (Trailhead); Disclosures and Consent Management in FSC (Trailhead); Personas and Permission Set Licenses for OmniStudio DocGen (help.salesforce.com)]. Key: OmniStudio DocGen is the primary FSC-native approach for compliance documents (disclosures, account statements, contracts) using Word/PPTX templates merged with DataRaptor-sourced data rendered to PDF; it is included with FSC Industries licensing but users still require separate DocGen permission set licenses per role — a common LLM error is claiming DocGen is fully included with no additional licensing steps. FSC-specific compliance patterns (FINRA disclosures, account statements) should use the Disclosures and Consent Management data model (AuthorizationForm + DataUseLegalBasis objects) driving document delivery, not raw OmniScript/DocGen templates alone; Document Builder (GA Winter '25+) is explicitly excluded from PCI compliance scope making it unsuitable for sensitive financial documents. Overlap: omnistudio/document-generation-omnistudio covers general DocGen mechanics — this skill focuses on FSC compliance-specific patterns, AuthorizationForm object usage, FINRA/GDPR regulatory disclosure workflows, and the server-side batch cap of 1000 documents/hour constraining statement runs. |
| DONE | fsc-integration-patterns-dev | FSC-specific integration: core banking sync, market data feeds, custodian integration, payment processing. NOT for generic integration. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [FSC Integrations API — Get Started (developer.salesforce.com); Salesforce Architects Integration Patterns Guide; MuleSoft FSC Setup Guide (docs.mulesoft.com)]. Key: FSC core banking and custodian sync (Schwab/Fidelity) primarily uses MuleSoft BIAN-canonical integration templates with Bulk API batch loads for daily FinancialAccount and FinancialHolding reconciliation; real-time custodian updates use the FSC Integrations API (Remote Call-In pattern) while CDC suits replication and Platform Events suit cross-app process orchestration. Critical gotcha: Rollup-by-Lookup triggers must be disabled for the integration user in Wealth Management Custom Settings before any bulk load of FinancialHolding or FinancialAccount — concurrent writes to the same parent cause row-lock failures; post-load recalculation should use DPE rather than re-enabling RBL in-band. Market data feeds updating CurrentValue on FinancialHolding must not use synchronous callouts from triggers — batch/scheduled Apex with post-load DPE aggregation is the correct pattern. |

### FSC × Data Role

> Domain folder: `data`

| Status | Skill Name | Description | Notes |
|--------|------------|-------------|-------|
| DONE | financial-account-migration | Financial account data migration: account types, holdings, positions, transaction history, balance data. NOT for standard account migration. | Researched 2026-04-10. Sources: [FSC Developer Guide Spring '26 (developer.salesforce.com); FinancialAccountTransaction Object Ref (developer.salesforce.com); FSC Core vs. Managed Package Migration Guide 2026 — VantagePoint].
